### [44] [Text Knows What, Tables Know When: Clinical Timeline Reconstruction via Retrieval-Augmented Multimodal Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15168)
*Sayantan Kumar,Shahriar Noroozizadeh,Juyong Kim,Jeremy C. Weiss*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多模态框架，通过将临床叙述中的语义信息与结构化EHR的时间锚点相结合，有效解决了临床时间轴重构中时间精度低与信息不完整的问题，显著提升了患者轨迹的重构效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床叙述包含丰富的语义但时间精度差，而结构化EHR数据虽然时间精确但信息缺失严重。现有方法难以整合两者的优势，导致无法准确重构复杂的患者临床时间轴，影响了疾病风险预测的准确性。

Method: 提出了一种基于检索增强的多模态对齐框架。该方法通过图结构将重构过程分为三步：1) 从临床叙述中提取核心锚点事件建立初始骨架；2) 将非核心事件相对定位；3) 利用检索到的结构化EHR记录作为外部时间证据对时间轴进行校准。模型基于指令微调的大语言模型（LLM）在MIMIC数据集上进行实验。

Result: 实验结果显示，该多模态流水线在i2m4基准测试中，相比单一模态方法，显著提升了绝对时间戳准确度（AULTC）和时间一致性，且未牺牲事件匹配率。此外，分析发现34.8%的临床事件仅存在于文本中，证实了跨模态对齐的必要性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了融合临床文本与结构化EHR数据的多模态方法，能够显著提升患者临床时间轴的重构精度和完整性，为后续的患者轨迹建模和风险预测提供了更可靠的临床基础。

Abstract: Reconstructing precise clinical timelines is essential for modeling patient trajectories and forecasting risk in complex, heterogeneous conditions like sepsis. While unstructured clinical narratives offer semantically rich and contextually complete descriptions of a patient's course, they often lack temporal precision and contain ambiguous event timing. Conversely, structured electronic health record (EHR) data provides precise temporal anchors but misses a substantial portion of clinically meaningful events. We introduce a retrieval-augmented multimodal alignment framework that bridges this gap to improve the temporal precision of absolute clinical timelines extracted from text. Our approach formulates timeline reconstruction as a graph-based multistep process: it first extracts central anchor events from narratives to build an initial temporal scaffold, places non-central events relative to this backbone, and then calibrates the timeline using retrieved structured EHR rows as external temporal evidence. Evaluated using instruction-tuned large language models on the i2m4 benchmark spanning MIMIC-III and MIMIC-IV, our multimodal pipeline consistently improves absolute timestamp accuracy (AULTC) and improves temporal concordance across nearly all evaluated models over unimodal text-only reconstruction, without compromising event match rates. Furthermore, our empirical gap analysis reveals that 34.8% of text-derived events are entirely absent from tabular records, demonstrating that aligning these modalities can produce a more temporally faithful and clinically informative reconstruction of patient trajectories than either source alone.

### [45] [Is Grep All You Need? How Agent Harnesses Reshape Agentic Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15184)
*Sahil Sen,Akhil Kasturi,Elias Lumer,Anmol Gulati,Vamse Kumar Subbiah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过实证研究发现，在 LLM 智能体任务中，相比于向量检索，基于 grep 的精确检索通常能提供更高的准确度，且智能体框架与工具调用方式的差异对最终性能影响巨大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对大型语言模型（LLM）智能体系统中检索策略、智能体架构与工具调用范式之间交互作用的系统性比较，特别是在面对无关噪声数据干扰以及不同工具输出呈现方式时，模型性能的变化机制尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 研究通过两个实验进行：实验1对比了 grep 和向量检索在多种智能体框架（Chronos 以及 Claude Code、Gemini CLI 等）下的性能，涵盖了行内工具结果与文件级工具结果两种呈现方式；实验2通过在查询中混入干扰性的对话历史，对比了 grep 与向量检索在噪声环境下的鲁棒性。

Result: 实验结果表明，在实验1中，grep 检索策略在大多数对比中优于向量检索；实验2发现，模型性能受所使用的智能体框架（harness）和工具调用风格影响巨大，即便底层数据一致，性能表现也会出现显著差异。整体而言，grep 在准确性方面展现出较强优势。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了在智能体工作流中，检索策略的选择、工具调用范式以及环境噪声对模型性能的影响显著。尽管目前向量检索在许多场景中被广泛使用，但针对特定代码库或文档集的检索任务，传统的 grep（精确匹配）在当前 Agent 工具调用架构下往往表现出更高的鲁棒性和准确性，且工具调用方式的选择对整体性能有决定性影响。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Model (LLM) agents have enabled complex agentic workflows where models autonomously retrieve information, call tools, and reason over large corpora to complete tasks on behalf of users. Despite the growing adoption of retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) in agentic search systems, existing literature lacks a systematic comparison of how retrieval strategy choice interacts with agent architecture and tool-calling paradigm. Important practical dimensions, including how tool outputs are presented to the model and how performance changes when searches must cope with more irrelevant surrounding text, remain under-explored in agent loops. This paper reports an empirical study organized into two experiments. Experiment 1 compares grep and vector retrieval on a 116-question sample from LongMemEval, using a custom agent harness (Chronos) and provider-native CLI harnesses (Claude Code, Codex, and Gemini CLI), for both inline tool results and file-based tool results that the model reads separately. Experiment 2 compares grep-only and vector-only retrieval while progressively mixing in additional unrelated conversation history, so that each query is embedded in more distracting material alongside the passages that matter. Across Chronos and the provider CLIs, grep generally yields higher accuracy than vector retrieval in our comparisons in experiment 1; at the same time, overall scores still depend strongly on which harness and tool-calling style is used, even when the underlying conversation data are the same.

### [46] [GAMBIT: A Three-Mode Benchmark for Adversarial Robustness in Multi-Agent LLM Collectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09027)
*Alexandre Le Mercier,Chris Develder,Thomas Demeester*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了多智能体系统（MAS）欺诈检测基准 GAMBIT，旨在解决现有研究忽视“自适应欺诈者”的问题。研究表明，仅依靠零样本评估无法有效应对进化型攻击，必须引入少样本重校准评估，以衡量防御系统应对动态演进威胁的真实鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统中，单一欺诈智能体可能彻底破坏整体协作效能，但现有研究多关注简单任务且忽视了欺诈者通过进化策略来规避检测器的“自适应”特性。因此，需要一个能够评估防御系统在面对演进型欺诈攻击时表现的基准。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含27,804个标记实例和240种共进化欺诈策略的基准测试集（GAMBIT）。
2. 利用国际象棋作为深度推理任务场景，并使用Gemini 3.1 Pro作为智能体基础。
3. 提出一种基于高效进化框架的自适应欺诈智能体，旨在协同干扰集体任务表现的同时保持极高的隐蔽性。
4. 设计了三种评估模式（零样本分布偏移检测及少样本重校准）及双重评分机制，用于评估欺诈检测器的鲁棒性与自适应能力。

Result: 1. 研发的自适应欺诈智能体在协作任务中表现出极强的破坏力，同时使检测器的检测性能仅维持在50.5%的F1分数。
2. 实验发现零样本评分具有误导性：两个零样本性能相近的检测器在面对新攻击时，少样本适应能力差距高达8倍。
3. 元学习（Meta-learned）变体在重校准模式下表现出快20倍的收敛速度，验证了该评估模式在揭示检测器真实能力上的重要性。

Conclusion: GAMBIT 是首个针对多智能体系统中自适应欺诈行为的评估基准。研究强调了零样本评估在面对自适应攻击时的局限性，并证实了重校准（recalibration）模式对于识别进化型威胁至关重要。该框架为构建更具鲁棒性的多智能体防御系统提供了有效的方法论支持。

Abstract: In multi-agent systems (MAS), a single deceptive agent can nullify all gains of an agentic AI collective and evade deployed defenses. However, existing adversarial studies on MAS target only shallow tasks and do not consider adaptive adversaries, which evolve their strategies to evade the very detectors trained to catch them. To address that gap, we introduce GAMBIT, a benchmark with three evaluation modes and two independent scores for evaluating imposter detectors: the first two modes measure zero-shot detection under increasing distribution shift, and a third recalibration mode measures how quickly a detector adapts to novel attacks from just 20 labeled examples. The benchmark comes with a dataset of 27,804 labeled instances spanning 240 co-evolved imposter strategies. Our contributions are threefold: (1) Using chess as a substrate deep reasoning problem and Gemini 3.1 Pro for agents, we release GAMBIT and its dataset to evaluate imposter detectors under realistic constraints against a stealthy adaptive imposter; (2) We introduce an adaptive imposter agent based on an efficient evolutionary framework, generalizable beyond chess, that collapses collective task performance while remaining essentially undetectable (50.5% F1-score with a Gemini-based detector); (3) We show that zero-shot evaluation can be highly misleading for adaptive adversaries: two detectors with near-identical zero-shot scores differ by 8x on few-shot adaptation, while the meta-learned variant converges 20x faster, a gap only visible in the recalibration mode. Altogether, GAMBIT provides the first multi-agent benchmark where adversarial attacks and defenses co-evolve, with an imposter framework generalizable beyond our use case, and promising techniques for fast recalibration in a rapidly evolving adversarial system. Code and data: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/gambit.

</details>


### [47] [ROK-FORTRESS: Measuring the Effect of Geopolitical Transcreation for National Security and Public Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14152)
*Michael S. Lee,Yash Maurya,Drew Rein,Bert Herring,Jonathan Nguyen,Kyungho Song,Udari Madhushani Sehwag,Jiyeon Cho,Kaustubh Deshpande,Yeongkyun Jang,Jiyeon Joo,Minn Seok Choi,Evi Fuelle,Christina Q Knight,Joseph Brandifino,Max Fenkell*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型的安全评估多依赖翻译后的基准测试，难以反映真实的全球化风险。现有研究缺乏对语言因素与地缘政治背景交互作用的深入分析，导致模型在处理高风险国家安全与公共安全（NSPS）问题时存在评估盲区。

Method: 研究构建了 ROK-FORTRESS 基准测试，采用“跨文化重构矩阵”（transcreation matrix）方法，通过控制语言（英语/韩语）和地缘政治背景（美国/韩国实体与机构）的排列组合，将语言变量与地缘政治变量解耦。此外，研究采用双用途良性对照组来量化过度拒绝现象，并使用经过校准的“LLM-as-a-judge”专家评分面板进行评估。

Result: 实验发现，模型在韩语环境下的安全抑制效应明显，且语言与地缘政治接地（grounding）之间存在复杂的交互作用。研究证实，将提示词转换为目标语言的同时保持地缘政治情境的一致性，能揭示传统翻译评估所忽略的风险偏见。不同模型表现出显著差异，部分模型在加入韩国地缘政治语境后，能够缓解纯语言驱动的过度抑制。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，针对大模型的安全评估不能仅依赖翻译测试。语言和地缘政治背景对模型的安全行为有独立且相互作用的影响。ROK-FORTRESS 提出的“跨文化重构矩阵”方法能够有效揭示这种复杂互动，并为开发更具包容性和准确性的全球安全评估框架提供了范式。

Abstract: Safety evaluations for large language models (LLMs) increasingly target high-stakes National Security and Public Safety (NSPS) risks, yet multilingual safety is typically assessed through translation-only benchmarks that preserve the underlying scenario, and empirical evidence of how language and geopolitical context interact remains limited to a narrow set of language pairs. We introduce \emph{ROK-FORTRESS} https://huggingface.co/datasets/ScaleAI/ROK-FORTRESS_public, a bilingual, culturally adversarial NSPS benchmark that uses the English--Korean language pair and U.S.--ROK geopolitical axis as a case study, separating the effects of language and geopolitical grounding via a \emph{transcreation matrix}: adversarial intents are evaluated under controlled combinations of (i) English versus Korean language and (ii) U.S.\ versus Korean entities, institutions, and operational details. Each adversarial prompt is paired with a dual-use benign counterpart to quantify over-refusal. Model responses are then scored using calibrated LLM-as-a-judge panels, applying our expert-crafted, prompt-specific binary rubrics.
  Across a dual-track set of frontier and Korean-optimized models, we find a consistent suppression effect in Korean variants and substantial model-to-model variation in how geopolitical grounding interacts with language. In many models, Korean grounding mitigates the Korean language-driven suppression -- with no model showing significant amplification in the other direction -- indicating that, at least in the English--Korean case, safety behavior is shaped by language-as-risk signals and context interactions that translation-only evaluations miss. The transcreation matrix methodology is designed to generalize to other language--culture pairs.

</details>


### [48] [Measuring and Mitigating Toxicity in Large Language Models: A Comprehensive Replication Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14087)
*Mokshit Surana,Archit Rathod,Akshaj Satishkumar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过复现分析指出，DExperts虽然能有效抑制显性毒性，但在应对隐性仇恨言论时存在鲁棒性短板，且高昂的推理延迟限制了其在实时场景中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在大规模语料训练中不可避免地吸收了毒性模式，导致“毒性退化”现象，即在无害提示下也可能产生有害输出。迫切需要一种既能保障模型安全性，又不牺牲模型实用性（无需重训练）的有效缓解策略。

Method: 本研究采用三阶段系统评估法：(1) 使用RealToxicityPrompts建立GPT-2模型的毒性基线；(2) 部署并评估DExperts（一种无需重训练的推理时引导解码技术）对显性毒性的缓解效果；(3) 使用ToxiGen数据集对DExperts进行对抗性测试，以评估其在隐性仇恨言论下的表现。

Result: 研究发现DExperts在显性毒性测试中实现了接近100%的安全性；然而，在对抗性的隐性仇恨言论（ToxiGen）面前表现出脆弱性，安全性降至98.5%。此外，该方法导致推理延迟增加了约10倍（从0.2秒增加到2.0秒），严重制约了其实时部署能力。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了DExperts方法在应对显性毒性内容时表现出色，但在处理隐性仇恨言论时存在鲁棒性漏洞，且在计算延迟方面存在显著瓶颈。研究强调了在追求大模型安全性的同时，必须平衡安全性、通用性和计算效率之间的矛盾，呼吁开发更高效、更具泛化能力的毒性防御方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs), when trained on web-scale corpora, inherently absorb toxic patterns from their training data. This leads to ``toxic degeneration'' where even innocuous prompts can trigger harmful outputs. This phenomenon poses significant risks for real-world deployments. Thus, necessitating effective mitigation strategies that should maintain model utility while ensuring safety. In this comprehensive replication study, we evaluate the efficacy of \textbf{DExperts} (Decoding-time Experts), which is an inference-time mitigation technique that steers generation without requiring model retraining. We structured our research into three systematic phases: (1) establishing baseline toxicity measurements using \textbf{RealToxicityPrompts} on standard GPT-2 models; then (2) implementing and evaluating DExperts to mitigate explicit toxicity; and finally (3) stress-testing the method against implicit hate speech using the adversarial \textbf{ToxiGen} dataset. Our empirical results confirm that while DExperts achieves near-perfect safety rates (100\%) on explicit toxicity benchmarks, it exhibits brittleness against adversarial, implicit hate speech, with safety rates dropping to 98.5\%. Furthermore, we quantify a critical trade-off. The method introduces a $\sim$10x latency penalty (from 0.2s to 2.0s per generation), posing challenges for real-time deployment scenarios. This study contributes to the growing body of work on AI safety by highlighting the robustness gap between explicit and implicit toxicity mitigation. We emphasize the need for more sophisticated approaches that generalize across diverse hate speech patterns without prohibitive computational costs.

</details>

### [49] [Towards the Next Frontier of LLMs, Training on Private Data: A Cross-Domain Benchmark for Federated Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13936)
*Daniel M. Jimenez-Gutierrez,Enrique Zuazua,Georgios Kellaris,Joaquin del Rio,Oleksii Sliusarenko,Xabi Uribe-Etxebarria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于联邦学习的框架，利用参数高效微调（PEFT）技术，在保护医疗和金融等领域私有数据隐私的前提下，成功实现了大型语言模型的跨机构协同优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型的进一步发展受限于数据，而最有价值的信息往往分布在受监管的医疗和金融机构中，这些数据因隐私、合规及分布异构（non-IID）等壁垒无法直接共享。本研究旨在通过联邦协作，在保护隐私的前提下解锁这些私有数据，以提升模型在特定领域的专业性能。

Method: 利用Sherpa.ai联邦学习平台，在不共享原始隐私数据的前提下，通过各节点协作共同微调共享的大型语言模型。实验评估了LoRA、QLoRA和IA3三种参数高效微调（PEFT）策略在非独立同分布（non-IID）数据环境下的性能。

Result: 实验结果表明，联邦微调的性能非常接近集中式训练，且显著优于单机构的隔离学习。同时，从绿色人工智能（Green AI）的角度看，QLoRA和IA3在保证性能的同时显著提升了计算效率。

Conclusion: 联邦微调（Federated Fine-Tuning）结合参数高效微调（PEFT）技术，是解决数据隐私和合规性限制下，实现大型语言模型领域知识适配的有效且可行的方案，特别是在医疗和金融等高度监管的领域。

Abstract: The recent success of large language models (LLMs) has been largely driven by vast public datasets. However, the next frontier for LLM development lies beyond public data. Much of the world's most valuable information is private, especially in highly regulated sectors such as healthcare and finance, where data include patient histories or customer communications. Unlocking this data could represent a major leap forward, enabling LLMs with deeper domain expertise and stronger real-world utility. Yet, these data cannot be shared because they are distributed across institutions and constrained by privacy, regulatory, and organizational barriers. Moreover, institutional datasets are typically non-independent and identically distributed (non-IID), differing across sites in population characteristics, data modalities, documentation patterns, and task-specific label distributions.
  In this paper, we demonstrate a practical approach to unlocking private and distributed institutional data for LLM adaptation through federated collaboration across data silos. Built on the Sherpa.ai Federated Learning platform, our framework enables nodes to jointly fine-tune a shared LLM without exchanging private data. We evaluate this approach through a cross-domain benchmark in healthcare and finance, using four closed-ended question answering and classification datasets: MedQA, MedMCQA, FPB, and FiQA-SA. We compare three parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) strategies-LoRA, QLoRA, and IA3-across pretrained backbones under non-IID settings reflecting institutional data heterogeneity. Our results show that federated fine-tuning performs close to centralized training and outperforms isolated single-institution learning. From a Green AI perspective, QLoRA and IA3 improve efficiency with limited accuracy degradation, supporting federated PEFT as a viable approach for adapting LLMs where data cannot be shared.

</details>


### [50] [WarmPrior: Straightening Flow-Matching Policies with Temporal Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13959)
*Sinjae Kang,Chanyoung Kim,Kaixin Wang,Li Zhao,Kimin Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 WarmPrior 的新型生成模型源分布设计，通过利用近期动作历史信息，改善了机器人控制模型中概率路径的平直度，从而显著提升了生成式策略的性能和训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的生成式机器人控制主要依赖标准的各向同性高斯分布作为扩散模型的源分布。研究者旨在通过优化源分布，解决生成轨迹弯曲、推理效率不高以及探索受限的问题，从而提升复杂机器人操作任务的成功率。

Method: 提出了一种名为“WarmPrior”的方法，用基于近期动作历史的、时间上扎根（temporally grounded）的分布替代了标准的独立同分布（i.i.d.）高斯分布作为生成模型的源分布。该方法不仅应用于行为克隆，还被用于先验空间强化学习以优化探索策略。

Result: 实验结果显示，WarmPrior 能够使概率路径显著变直（类似于矩流中的最优传输耦合），在多项机器人操作任务中提升了成功率，并提高了先验空间强化学习的样本效率和最终性能。

Conclusion: 研究表明，源分布的选择是生成式机器人控制中一个关键且被低估的设计维度。通过引入基于时间序列动作历史的“WarmPrior”，可以显著提升轨迹平直度，从而改进扩散/流匹配模型在机器人操作任务中的性能及探索效率。

Abstract: Generative policies based on diffusion and flow matching have become a dominant paradigm for visuomotor robotic control. We show that replacing the standard Gaussian source distribution with WarmPrior, a simple temporally grounded prior constructed from readily available recent action history, consistently improves success rates on robotic manipulation tasks. We trace this gain to markedly straighter probability paths, echoing the effect of optimal-transport couplings in Rectified Flow. Beyond standard behavior cloning, WarmPrior also reshapes the exploration distribution in prior-space reinforcement learning, improving both sample efficiency and final performance. Collectively, these results identify the source distribution as an important and underexplored design axis in generative robot control.

### [51] [Neural Fields for NV-Center Inverse Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13988)
*Zhixuan Zhao,Tao Zhong,Yixun Hu,Nathalie P. de Leon,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对量子传感中的非线性反问题，提出了NeTMY神经场框架。通过引入物理精确的偶极子前向模型和改进的优化策略，有效解决了传统方法中常见的定位偏差与“中心坍缩”问题，提升了对稀疏源磁噪声谱的重构性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的反问题求解方法（基于人工设计的正则化或监督学习）在面对非线性、谱耦合且物理敏感的系统时表现欠佳。特别是在氮-空位（NV）中心磁噪声传感任务中，现有的标量近似模型会导致“中心坍缩”失效模式，难以准确重建稀疏自旋源的分布。

Method: 提出了NeTMY，一种无需摊销的坐标神经场（coordinate neural field）。其核心在于：1. 采用了更精确的张量幂和偶极子算子作为微分前向模型；2. 结合了退火位置编码（annealed positional encoding）、多尺度优化、稀疏/门控机制以及谱保真度损失函数。这种参数化方式有效地平滑并重新分布了梯度更新。

Result: 在合成数据基准测试中，NeTMY在定位精度和分布指标上均优于现有方法。机制实验进一步表明，该方法通过参数化策略改变了梯度更新路径，成功缓解了优化过程中的中心坍缩问题，在物理一致性与重构质量之间取得了平衡。

Conclusion: NeTMY方法有效地解决了NV中心量子传感中的反问题挑战。通过引入物理一致性的前向模型和坐标神经场优化，该方法克服了传统优化中常见的“中心坍缩”缺陷，证明了物理感知神经反问题框架在复杂量子传感任务中的优越性。

Abstract: Inverse problems in scientific sensing are often solved with either hand-designed regularizers or supervised networks trained on simulated labels, yet both can fail when the forward model is nonlinear, spectrally coupled, and physically delicate. We study this issue for noise sensing based on nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond, where a quantum sensor measures magnetic-noise spectra generated by sparse spin sources. We show that replacing a common scalar/coherent forward approximation with a tensor power-summed dipolar operator changes the inverse landscape and exposes a center-collapse failure mode in free-density optimization. We propose NeTMY, an amortization-free coordinate neural field coupled to the differentiable NV forward model, with annealed positional encoding, multiscale optimization, sparsity/gating, and spectrum-fidelity losses. Across sparse synthetic reconstructions generated by the corrected operator, NeTMY achieves the best localization and distributional metrics in the tested benchmark. Mechanism experiments show that NeTMY does not directly execute the raw density-space gradient; its parameterization smooths and redistributes updates, mitigating the center-collapse pathology. These results position NV quantum sensing as a useful testbed for physics-faithful neural inverse problems.

</details>


### [52] [Support Before Frequency in Discrete Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13999)
*Adrian Müller,Antoine Gonon,Zebang Shen,Ya-Ping Hsieh,Niao He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究揭示了离散扩散模型（如掩码语言模型）的一种普遍学习行为：模型会优先学习数据的结构性支撑（如语法正确性），随后才逐步精确化地学习数据的频率分布。这一结论通过反向去噪过程的数学分解与实验验证得到了支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散扩散模型在语言建模中表现优异，但目前尚不清楚其去噪目标如何组织学习过程。研究者旨在探索这些模型在学习过程中如何权衡全局分布与局部特征，特别是在处理离散数据时，数据结构（支撑集）与数据分布（频率）的获取是否存在先后顺序。

Method: 研究通过对均匀扩散（uniform diffusion）和吸收扩散（absorbing diffusion，即掩码扩散）进行数学建模与分析。研究者证明了在小噪声状态下，反向去噪过程可以分解为“主要尺度”（决定是否趋向数据支撑集）和“精细系数”（决定内部概率分布）两个部分，并对比了不同扩散机制下的编辑行为特征（如有效性提升、维持或恶化）。此外，通过掩码语言模型实验和合成正则语言任务对上述理论预测进行了验证。

Result: 实验结果表明，在模型训练过程中，支撑集定位（support-localization）的习得早于支撑集内部的频率排序。同时，吸收扩散模型在向数据支撑集移动方面展现出更强的导向性，实验数据有力支持了研究者关于学习速率分离和机制差异的理论预测。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论证明与实验验证揭示了离散扩散模型学习数据的内在机制：模型遵循“先学习数据支撑集（结构/语法），后学习数据频率（分布细节）”的学习模式。这一发现为理解离散扩散模型在语言建模中的表现提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are increasingly competitive for language modeling, yet it remains unclear how their denoising objectives organize learning. Although these objectives target the full data distribution, we show that the exact reverse process induces a hierarchy between coarse support information and finer frequency information. For uniform and absorbing (a.k.a. masking) diffusion, we prove that, in the small-noise regime of the final denoising steps, each single-token reverse edit decomposes into a leading scale, determined by whether it moves toward the data support (e.g., grammatically valid sentences), and a finer coefficient, determining relative probabilities within the same scale. Thus, recovering validity structure only requires learning the correct order of magnitude of reverse probabilities, whereas recovering data frequencies requires coefficient-level estimation. The separation is mechanism-dependent: uniform diffusion exhibits a trichotomy into validity-improving, validity-preserving, and validity-worsening edits, while absorbing diffusion places its leading-order mass on validity-improving moves. Experiments on a masked language diffusion model and synthetic regular-language tasks support these predictions: support-localization emerges earlier than within-support frequency ranking, and the contrast between uniform and absorbing diffusion matches the predicted rate separation. Together, our results suggest that discrete diffusion models learn data support before data frequencies.

</details>


### [53] [Dywave: Event-Aligned Dynamic Tokenization for Heterogeneous IoT Sensing Signal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14014)
*Tomoyoshi Kimura,Denizhan Kara,Jinyang Li,Hongjue Zhao,Yigong Hu,Yizhuo Chen,Xiaomin Ouyang,Shengzhong Liu,Tarek Abdelzaher*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Dywave，一种面向物联网传感信号的动态Token化框架，通过小波分解与语义边界识别实现信号的紧凑表达，在大幅提升计算效率的同时显著增强了模型性能与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网系统中的传感信号通常具有非平稳和多尺度特性，传统的固定Token化方法难以捕捉其内在的时间结构和物理事件语义，导致处理效率低下且难以有效表征复杂信号。

Method: 提出了一种名为Dywave的动态Token化框架，核心技术包括：利用基于小波分析的层级分解技术处理非平稳信号；通过识别与物理事件对应的语义时间边界来划分Token；自适应压缩冗余时间区间，在保持时间相关性的同时构建紧凑的输入表示。

Result: 在五个物联网传感数据集（涵盖活动识别、压力评估及物体检测）上的实验表明，Dywave相比现有先进方法提升了最高12%的分类准确率，并将序列模型的输入Token长度减少了最高75%，同时表现出更强的领域适应能力。

Conclusion: Dywave框架通过动态调整Token化策略，有效解决了物联网传感信号处理中的非平稳性和多尺度问题。该方法在显著降低计算开销的同时提升了模型精度与鲁棒性，为物联网智能传感信号的高效处理提供了一种通用且有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Internet of Things (IoT) systems continuously collect heterogeneous sensing signals from ubiquitous sensors to support intelligent applications such as human activity analysis, emotion monitoring, and environmental perception. These signals are inherently non-stationary and multi-scale, posing unique challenges for standard tokenization techniques. This paper proposes Dywave, a dynamic tokenization framework for IoT sensing signals that constructs compact input representations aligned with intrinsic temporal structures and underlying physical events. Dywave leverages wavelet-based hierarchical decomposition, identifies meaningful temporal boundaries corresponding to underlying semantic events, and adaptively compresses redundant intervals while preserving temporal coherence. Extensive evaluations on five real-world IoT sensing datasets across activity recognition, stress assessment, and nearby object detection demonstrate that Dywave outperforms state-of-the-art methods by up to 12% in accuracy, while improving computational efficiency by reducing input token lengths by up to 75% across mainstream sequence models. Moreover, Dywave exhibits improved robustness to domain shifts and varying sequence lengths.

</details>


### [54] [R2R2: Robust Representation for Intensive Experience Reuse via Redundancy Reduction in Self-Predictive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14026)
*Sanghyeob Song,Donghyeok Lee,Jinsik Kim,Sungroh Yoon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对强化学习在高更新数据比（UTD）下的过拟合问题，本文提出 R2R2 正则化方法，通过修正 SPL 的非中心化目标函数，显著提升了表示学习的稳定性与数据利用效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数据稀缺的真实机器人强化学习场景中，高强度的重用数据会导致严重的过拟合现象。现有研究多集中于批判者（critic）偏置，却忽视了高更新数据比（UTD）环境下自预测学习（SPL）在表示层面的不稳定性。因此，作者旨在寻找一种能够减少表示冗余并提升稳定性的正则化手段。

Method: 本文提出了“冗余缩减的稳健表示”（R2R2）方法。首先，在理论上分析了标准零中心化与 SPL 谱属性之间的冲突；其次，设计了一个非中心化的正则化目标函数来优化表示学习；最后，通过将该机制集成到 TD7 及扩展版 SimbaV2-SPL 中进行验证。

Result: 实验在 11 个连续控制任务上进行，结果显示 R2R2 能有效缓解过拟合。在 UTD 比率为 20 的设置下，R2R2 将 TD7 的性能提升了约 22%；同时，该方法与 SimbaV2-SPL 结合后进一步提升了性能，刷新了相关任务的最高性能纪录（SOTA）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 R2R2 方法通过引入非中心化的正则化目标，成功解决了自预测学习（SPL）在高更新数据比（UTD）场景下的表示不稳定性与过拟合问题，为强化学习在数据稀缺领域的高效应用提供了稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: For reinforcement learning in data-scarce domains like real-world robotics, intensive data reuse enhances efficiency but induces overfitting. While prior works focus on critic bias, representation-level instability in Self-Predictive Learning (SPL) under high Update-to-Data (UTD) regimes remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction (R2R2), a regularization method within SPL. We theoretically identify that standard zero-centering conflicts with SPL's spectral properties and design a non-centered objective accordingly. We verify R2R2 on SPL-native algorithms like TD7. Furthermore, to demonstrate its orthogonality to prior advancements, we extend the state-of-the-art SimbaV2, which originally lacks SPL, by integrating a tailored SPL module, termed SimbaV2-SPL. Experiments across 11 continuous control tasks confirm that R2R2 effectively mitigates overfitting; specifically, at a UTD ratio of 20, it improves TD7 by ~22% and provides additional gains on top of SimbaV2-SPL, which itself establishes a new state-of-the-art. The code can be found at: https://github.com/songsang7/R2R2

</details>


### [55] [Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention: Learning When to Write by Predicting Future Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14037)
*Gergely Szilvasy,Manuel Faysse,Maria Lomeli,Matthijs Douze,Pierre-Emmanuel Mazaré,Loïc Cabannes,Wen-tau Yih,Hervé Jégou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SP-KV 通过轻量级预测器动态剪枝不重要的键值对，实现了 KV 缓存的大幅度压缩，在显著降低内存需求和提升解码速度的同时，几乎不损失模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代大语言模型和智能体范式下，处理超长序列导致 Transformer 的 KV 缓存内存占用与带宽成为性能瓶颈。作者旨在开发一种能够在保持生成质量的同时，动态压缩长上下文 KV 缓存的方法，以提升推理效率。

Method: 提出了一种自剪枝键值注意力机制（SP-KV）。该方法通过一个轻量级的效用预测器对每个 KV 对进行打分；保留最近的 KV 对以保证局部注意力，而对历史 KV 对根据预测的效用值进行阈值过滤，仅保留重要的 KV 对进入全局注意力缓存。模型与预测器通过下一个词预测损失进行联合端到端训练。

Result: SP-KV 实现了 3 到 10 倍的 KV 缓存压缩率，且随着序列增长，压缩效果更佳。在保持验证损失几乎无损的同时，在各项下游任务中表现优异，显著提升了推理速度并降低了内存开销。此外，该方法还识别出了特定的层级和头级稀疏性模式。

Conclusion: SP-KV 为处理超长上下文提供了一种高效、动态的键值缓存压缩方案。研究表明，通过预测 KV 对的效用进行稀疏化，可以在不牺牲模型性能的前提下显著降低内存占用，并揭示了模型注意力机制中存在的层级与头级稀疏模式，为未来高效 Transformer 架构的设计提供了参考。

Abstract: Under modern test-time compute and agentic paradigms, language models process ever-longer sequences. Efficient text generation with transformer architectures is increasingly constrained by the Key-Value cache memory footprint and bandwidth. To address this limitation, we introduce Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention (SP-KV), a mechanism designed to predict future KV utility in order to reduce the size of the long-term KV cache. This strategy operates at a fine granularity: a lightweight utility predictor scores each key-value pair, and while recent KVs are always available via a local window, older pairs are written in the cache and used in global attention only if their predicted utility surpasses a given threshold. The LLM and the utility predictor are trained jointly end-to-end exclusively through next-token prediction loss, and are adapted from pretrained LLM checkpoints.
  Rather than enforcing a fixed compression ratio, SP-KV performs dynamic sparsification: the mechanism adapts to the input and typically reduces the KV cache size by a factor of $3$ to $10\times$, longer sequences often being more compressible. This leads to vast improvements in memory usage and decoding speed, with little to no degradation of validation loss nor performance on a broad set of downstream tasks. Beyond serving as an effective KV-cache reduction mechanism, our method reveals structured layer- and head-specific sparsity patterns that we can use to guide the design of hybrid local-global attention architectures.

</details>


### [56] [Reliability-Gated Source Anchoring for Continual Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14063)
*Vikash Singh,Debargha Ganguly,Weicong Chen,Sabyasachi Sahoo,Sreehari Sankar,Biyao Zhang,Mohsen Harir,Shouren Wang,Osama Zafar,Christian Gagné,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 CTTA 中盲目依赖不可靠源模型导致的性能崩溃问题，本文提出了 RMemSafe 方法，通过熵门控机制在源模型失效时自动剥离锚定约束，显著提升了模型在持续极端分布偏移下的稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在持续测试时间适应（CTTA）场景中，现有方法过度依赖冻结的源检查点进行锚定。当源模型在面对严重分布偏移（如 CCC-Hard 数据集）而表现极差（精度仅 1.3%）时，强制锚定会导致模型性能严重退化，即所谓的“盲目锚定”失效模式。

Method: RMemSafe 算法：一种改进的可靠性门控方法。它利用冻结源模型的归一化预测熵作为门控信号，当源模型预测趋于均匀分布（即源模型不可靠）时，自动削弱或关闭源锚定（Anchor）和一致性过滤（Agreement filter），并将目标函数转换为源无关的备用模式（仅保留基础损失和边缘校准）。

Result: 在 9 个匹配分割的持续腐蚀（continual-corruption）单元格中，RMemSafe 在 8 个单元格中达到了最低误差。相比于原有的 ROID+ASR 方法，在 ResNet-50 和 ViT-B/16 上分别提升了 1.05 和 0.48 个百分点，并表现出更平滑的性能衰减斜率。

Conclusion: 本文提出了 RMemSafe 方法，通过引入基于熵的可靠性门控机制，有效解决了持续测试时间适应（CTTA）中“盲目锚定”导致模型性能下降的问题，实现了在源模型不可靠时的优雅降级。

Abstract: Continual test-time adaptation (CTTA) updates a pretrained model online on an unlabeled, non-stationary stream while anchoring it to a frozen source checkpoint. This anchor is useful only when the source remains reliable. On CCC-Hard, however, a ResNet-50 source falls to approximately $1.3\%$ top-$1$ accuracy, while existing source-anchored CTTA methods continue applying the same anchor strength. We call this failure mode blind anchoring and propose RMemSafe, a reliability-gated extension of ROID that uses the frozen source's normalized predictive entropy to attenuate all explicit source-coupled uses in the objective. When the source posterior approaches uniformity, the gate closes: the source anchor and agreement filter vanish, and the objective reduces to a source-agnostic fallback comprising ROID's base losses plus marginal calibration. Combined with ASR, RMemSafe achieves the lowest error on $8$ of $9$ matched-split continual-corruption cells and is the best reset-based method on all $9$, improving ROID+ASR by $1.05$~pp on ResNet-50 and $0.48$~pp on ViT-B/16. A controlled source-degradation sweep shows a $1.13{\times}$ shallower harm slope than ROID+ASR, consistent with the graceful-decay prediction. The entropy gate detects high-entropy source collapse, not confidently wrong low-entropy sources; this scope is explicitly evaluated and discussed.

</details>


### [57] [SurF: A Generative Model for Multivariate Irregular Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14069)
*Mohammad R. Rezaei,Tejas Balaji,Rahul G. Krishnan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SurF 是一种用于不规则事件流的生成模型，它通过时间重缩放定理将事件序列映射为指数噪声，实现了高效的跨数据集训练与长序列建模，是通向异步事件流基础模型的重要进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有处理不规则采样多变量事件流的方法存在局限性：基于 Token 的方法在处理时间间隔差异巨大的序列时效果不佳，而神经时间点过程方法受限于窗口级数值积分的计算瓶颈。因此，研究者旨在开发一种能跨异构数据集训练、具备高效扩展性并能进行多数据集预训练的通用生成模型。

Method: 1. 利用时间重缩放定理（TRT）构建事件序列与 i.i.d. 单位速率指数噪声之间的可学习双射；2. 提出了三种高效的累积强度参数化方法，以处理长序列；3. 构建了基于 Transformer 的编码器，支持多数据集预训练。

Result: 在六个真实世界基准数据集上，SurF 在 Earthquake、Retweet 和 Taobao 数据集上实现了最优的时间预测 RMSE；在严格的留一法验证协议下，SurF 在 6 个数据集中的 5 个表现优于所有传统及神经自回归基准，且在 Amazon 和 Earthquake 上全面领先。

Conclusion: SurF 成功地利用时间重缩放定理实现了异构事件流的统一建模，证明了其作为异步事件流基础模型（Foundation Model）的潜力，并在多项基准测试中展现出超越传统及神经自回归基准的卓越性能。

Abstract: Irregularly sampled multivariate event streams remain a stubbornly difficult modality for generative modeling: tokenization-based approaches break down when inter-event intervals vary by orders of magnitude, and neural temporal point processes are bottlenecked by window-level numerical quadrature. We (i) propose SurF, a generative model that uses the Time Rescaling Theorem (TRT) as a learnable bijection between event sequences and i.i.d.\ unit-rate exponential noise, enabling a single model to be trained across heterogeneous event-stream datasets; (ii) three efficient parameterizations of the cumulative intensity that scale to long sequences; and (iii) a Transformer-based encoder for multi-dataset pretraining. On six real-world benchmarks, SurF achieves the best reported time RMSE on Earthquake, Retweet, and Taobao, and is within trial-level noise of the strongest specialist on the remaining three. Under a strict leave-one-out protocol, the held-out checkpoint beats every classical and neural-autoregressive baseline on 5/6 datasets and beats every baseline on Amazon and Earthquake, an initial step toward foundation models over asynchronous event streams.

### [58] [AttnGen: Attention-Guided Saliency Learning for Interpretable Genomic Sequence Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14073)
*Rayhaneh Shabani Nia,Ali Karkehabadi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AttnGen 是一种新型的注意力引导训练框架，通过在训练过程中自动筛选并掩码无关的基因组序列片段，在显著提升分类准确率和模型稳定性的同时，实现了更出色的模型可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管深度学习在基因组序列分类任务中表现优异，但其模型内部的“黑盒”特性使得难以将预测结果与具体的生物学意义关联起来。为了解决这一问题，研究者旨在开发一种能够在训练阶段直接整合可解释性引导的框架，从而提升模型对关键生物特征的捕捉能力。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 AttnGen 的训练框架，其核心在于将可解释性嵌入优化过程。该方法通过注意力机制计算核苷酸级别的贡献度得分，并在训练过程中逐步掩码（抑制）低贡献的序列位置，迫使模型在学习过程中仅依赖于最具有信息量的紧凑序列片段。

Result: 在 human_or_worm 基准测试中，AttnGen 达到了 96.73% 的验证准确率，优于传统 CNN 基准（95.83%），并表现出更快的收敛速度和稳定性。扰动分析实验证实了模型对高贡献度位置的高度依赖：移除高显著性核苷酸后，模型准确率大幅下降，证明模型确实捕捉到了功能相关的生物信号。此外，研究发现掩码 10%-20% 的序列位置可获得性能与可解释性的最佳平衡。

Conclusion: AttnGen 通过注意力引导的掩码机制成功实现了模型性能与可解释性的双重提升。研究表明，该方法不仅能帮助模型更精准地聚焦于生物学相关的序列片段，还能通过减少噪声特征的干扰来增强模型的鲁棒性和收敛速度。这一成果为处理复杂基因组序列的可解释性建模提供了一种有效且通用的范式。

Abstract: Deep neural networks have achieved strong performance in genomic sequence classification; however, relating their predictions to biologically meaningful sequence patterns remains challenging. In this work, we present AttnGen, an attention-guided training framework that embeds interpretability directly into the optimization process. AttnGen computes nucleotide-level importance scores using an attention mechanism and progressively suppresses low-contribution positions during training. This encourages the model to focus its predictions on a compact set of informative regions while reducing reliance on noisy sequence elements. We evaluate AttnGen on the standardized demo_human_or_worm benchmark, a binary classification task over 200-nucleotide sequences. With moderate masking, AttnGen achieves a validation accuracy of 96.73%, outperforming a conventional CNN baseline with 95.83% accuracy, while also exhibiting faster convergence and improved training stability. To assess whether the learned importance scores reflect functionally relevant signal, we conduct perturbation-based analysis by removing high-saliency nucleotides. This causes accuracy to drop from 96.9% to near chance level on a 3,000-sequence evaluation set, indicating that the model relies on a relatively small subset of informative positions. Our analysis shows that masking 10--20% of positions provides the most favorable trade-off between predictive performance and interpretability. These results suggest that attention-guided masking not only improves classification performance but also reshapes how models distribute importance across sequence positions. Although this study focuses on short genomic sequences, the proposed approach may extend to more complex interpretable sequence modeling settings.

### [59] [Fair and Calibrated Toxicity Detection with Robust Training and Abstention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14074)
*Mokshit Surana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了毒性分类中公平性的多维复杂性，指出训练干预和后处理机制存在深层耦合，单纯优化排名指标可能掩盖校准偏差和弃权机制带来的不公平，强调必须采用多轴框架进行评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前毒性分类公平性研究往往将训练干预与后处理安全机制割裂开来，导致难以全面评估模型在排名、校准和弃权三个核心轴上的公平表现，且未能有效应对潜在的隐性不公平问题。

Method: 对比了经验风险最小化（ERM）、实例级重加权和分组分布鲁棒优化（Group DRO）三种训练方法，并结合温度缩放、基于置信度的弃权及按身份阈值优化等后处理机制；评估指标包括子群AUC、BPSN/BNSP AUC、误差差距及按子群划分的期望校准误差（ECE）。

Result: 研究发现：（1）校准差异是隐性的公平性违规，ERM虽聚合校准良好但各子群间存在显著差异；（2）训练干预未能消除差异，仅改变了表现形式（如重加权虽提升排名但扩大了校准差距，Group DRO消除了校准差异却导致全局校准失效）；（3）后处理方法受训练模式限制，如基于置信度的弃权在DRO下表现极差；（4）弃权机制本身存在偏见，对背景内容比对涉及身份的内容更有利。

Conclusion: 作者认为毒性分类中的公平性必须在一个包含排名、校准和弃权的多轴框架下进行综合评估。仅仅关注聚合排名指标是不够的，不同训练干预方法会导致截然不同的失效模式，进而引发严重的现实世界公平性隐患。

Abstract: Fairness in toxicity classification involves three integrated axes: ranking, calibration, and abstention. Training-time interventions and post-hoc safety mechanisms cannot be evaluated independently because the former determines the efficacy of the latter. We compare Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM), instance-level reweighting, and Group DRO across these axes, combined with temperature scaling, confidence-based abstention, and per-identity threshold optimization. Evaluation uses subgroup AUC, BPSN/BNSP AUC, error gaps, and per-subgroup Expected Calibration Error (ECE) with bootstrap CIs ($n = 1000$).
  We report four findings. (1) Calibration disparity is a hidden fairness violation. ERM has near-perfect aggregate calibration ($0.013$) but is significantly miscalibrated across all identity subgroups ($+0.029$ to $+0.134$). (2) Training interventions reshape rather than eliminate disparity. Reweighted ERM improves ranking (BPSN AUC $+0.06$ to $+0.12$) but worsens the calibration-fairness gap by up to $+0.232$. Group DRO eliminates calibration disparity but only by becoming uniformly miscalibrated globally (ECE $0.118$). (3) Post-hoc methods inherit training failure modes. Temperature scaling fails because miscalibration is non-uniform. Confidence-based abstention works under ERM but breaks under DRO, where the risk-coverage curve rises with deferral. (4) Abstention itself is unfair. Confidence-based deferral helps background content far more than identity-mentioning content. We argue that SRAI fairness requires a multi-axis framework: methods that differ only in aggregate ranking can differ sharply in failure modes that determine real-world harm.

Abstract: Fast Healthcare Interoperability Resources (FHIR) is the dominant standard for interoperable exchange of healthcare data. Answering clinically meaningful questions over FHIR requires agents to perform multi-step reasoning, filtering, and aggregation across multiple resource types. We study this problem in the context of FHIR-AgentBench, a benchmark for realistic question answering over real-world hospital data, and frame reasoning on FHIR as a sequential decision-making problem over a queryable structured graph. We implement a multi-turn CodeAct agent and post-train it with reinforcement learning using a custom harness and tools. A LLM Judge provides execution-grounded rewards. Compared to prompt-based, closed-model baselines, RL post-training improves performance while enforcing data-integrity constraints. Empirically, our approach improves answer correctness from 50% (o4-mini) to 77% on FHIR-AgentBench using a smaller and cheaper Qwen3-8B model. We present an end-to-end post-training pipeline (environment building, harness construction, model training and custom evaluation) that reliably improves multi-turn reasoning over structured clinical graphs.

  <summary>Details</summary>

In this work, we provide a non-asymptotic sample complexity analysis for learning the structure of exponential families of polynomials with score matching. The derived sample bounds show a polynomial dependence on the model dimension. These bounds are the first of its kind, as all prior work has shown only asymptotic bounds on the sample complexity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Channel state information (CSI) provides a widely available sensing modality for human and environment perception, but existing CSI sensing models usually rely on task-specific supervised training and require substantial labeled data for each task, device, user, or environment. This limits their scalability in practical deployments where unlabeled CSI is abundant but labeled data is costly to collect. In this paper, we present CSI-JEPA, a self-supervised predictive representation learning framework for label-efficient, multi-task Wi-Fi sensing. CSI-JEPA learns reusable temporal-spectral representations from unlabeled CSI samples by predicting latent features of masked channel regions from visible context. To better match the physical structure of CSI, CSI-JEPA tokenizes channel-response amplitude windows along the time and subcarrier dimensions. It then introduces a channel variation-aware masking strategy that samples predictive targets from regions with stronger local temporal and subcarrier-domain variations. After pretraining, the encoder is frozen and used as a backbone, with lightweight task-specific adapters added for downstream sensing tasks. We evaluate CSI-JEPA on seven real-world Wi-Fi sensing tasks spanning diverse objectives and deployment settings. The results show that CSI-JEPA improves downstream sensing performance over competitive baselines, achieving up to 10.64 percentage points mean accuracy gain over state-of-the-art supervised Transformer and matched-budget label savings of up to 98.0%.

### [65] [LLMs Know When They Know, but Do Not Act on It: A Metacognitive Harness for Test-time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14186)
*Qi Cao,Yufan Wang,Peijia Qin,Shuhao Zhang,Pengtao Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将大语言模型的元认知监控能力转化为推理控制接口的框架，通过在推理前后进行自我评估并据此进行动态决策，在不微调模型的前提下显著提升了推理任务的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在解决问题前后表现出一定的自我监控能力（即估计成功率或判断正确性），但这些信号通常被孤立地测量，未能被有效地用于指导推理过程。本文旨在探讨如何将这种潜在的元认知能力转化为有效的测试时推理控制手段。

Method: 研究者借鉴认知心理学中的纳尔逊-纳伦斯（Nelson-Narens）理论，设计了一个元认知控制框架：在推理前要求模型进行“知晓感”（FOK）评估，在推理后进行“学习判断”（JOL）评估。该框架将这些信号转化为控制推理过程的接口，通过动态决定是采纳当前答案、基于反馈重试，还是合并多个尝试结果，从而优化最终输出。

Result: 在无需任何参数更新或特定任务微调的情况下，该方法使 Claude Sonnet-4.6 的基准测试准确率从 48.3% 提升至 56.9%，并在 HLE-Verified、LiveCodeBench v6 和 R-Bench-V 三个主要基准测试中超越了排行榜上的现有最佳模型。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型（LLM）具备潜在的元认知能力，通过显式的控制框架（Metacognitive Harness），可以在不进行参数微调的情况下，显著提升模型在文本、代码和多模态推理任务中的性能。这证明了将监控与推理分离是增强模型推理能力的有效途径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often expose useful signals of self-monitoring: before solving a problem, they can estimate whether they are likely to succeed, and after solving it, they can judge whether their answer is likely to be correct. However, these signals are typically measured or elicited in isolation, rather than used to control inference. In this work, we ask whether LLMs possess latent metacognitive ability that can be turned into effective test-time control. Inspired by the Nelson--Narens theory from cognitive psychology, we propose a metacognitive harness that separates monitoring from reasoning. For each problem, the model first reports a pre-solve feeling-of-knowing (FOK) signal; after each solve attempt, it reports a post-solve judgment-of-learning (JOL) signal. Rather than treating these signals as passive confidence estimates, the harness turns them into an explicit control interface for reasoning: it decides when to trust the current solution, when to retry with compact metacognitive feedback, and when to pass multiple attempts to a final aggregator. Across text, code, and multimodal reasoning benchmarks, our harness substantially improves a fixed Claude Sonnet-4.6 base model without parameter updates or benchmark-specific fine-tuning. On the evaluated public benchmark snapshots, it raises pooled accuracy from 48.3 to 56.9 and exceeds the strongest listed leaderboard entries on the three primary evaluation settings: HLE-Verified, LiveCodeBench v6, and R-Bench-V. These results suggest that strong LLMs may already possess useful metacognitive ability, but require an explicit control harness to act on it during reasoning.

### [66] [How to Scale Mixture-of-Experts: From muP to the Maximally Scale-Stable Parameterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14200)
*Leena Chennuru Vankadara,Moritz Haas,Luke Hayward,Sebastian Bordt,Alessandro Breccia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文针对MoE模型缺乏系统性扩展理论的问题，提出了基于动态平均场理论的MSSP参数化方案，解决了传统方法在规模扩展时的稳定性与性能迁移难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流的大规模语言模型多采用混合专家（MoE）架构，但缺乏针对模型宽度（N）、专家宽度（Ne）、专家数量（M）、稀疏度（K）和深度（L）等超参数的理论扩展准则，导致在模型规模化过程中难以保证训练稳定性和性能提升。

Method: 1. 构建了针对MoE训练动力学的动态平均场理论（DMFT），涵盖三种不同的扩展范式（协同扩展N与Ne、协同扩展N与M/K、全比例扩展）。
2. 在此框架下推导了原始的最大化更新（μP）参数化，并指出其在扩展中的稳定性缺陷。
3. 提出了“最大尺度稳定性”原则，据此导出了新的最大尺度稳定参数化（MSSP）。
4. 通过实验验证了MSSP在不同扩展范式下的学习率迁移能力和性能表现。

Result: 1. 证明了传统的μP参数化无法在MoE架构中实现鲁棒的学习率迁移或单调性能提升。
2. 成功推导出适用于三种扩展范式的MSSP参数化方案。
3. 实验表明，MSSP能够有效实现学习率的跨尺度迁移，并确保模型性能随规模增加呈现单调增长，为MoE扩展提供了完整的理论指导。

Conclusion: 该研究通过提出最大尺度稳定性原则（MSSP），修正了现有参数化方案在MoE模型扩展中的局限性。MSSP不仅实现了稳定的超参数跨尺度迁移，还保证了模型性能随规模增加的单调提升，为MoE架构的系统化扩展提供了完整的理论框架。

Abstract: Recent frontier large language models predominantly rely on Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures. Despite empirical progress, there is still no principled understanding of how hyperparameters should scale with network width $N$, expert width $N_e$, number of experts $M$, sparsity $K$, and depth $L$ to ensure both stability and optimal performance at scale. We take a principled step toward resolving this gap by analyzing three different scaling regimes: (I) co-scaling $N\asymp N_e$, (II) co-scaling $N\asymp M\asymp K$, and (III) full proportional scaling of $N, N_e, M$, and $K$. For each regime, we develop a novel Dynamical Mean Field Theory (DMFT) description of the limiting training dynamics of MoEs that provides a formal foundation for our analysis. Within this framework, we derive the unique parameterization for SGD and Adam satisfying all maximal-update ($μ$) desiderata. We then show that the resulting $μ$P prescription does not reliably induce monotonic improvement with scale or robust learning-rate transfer. We trace these pathologies to scale-dependent observables in the aggregation dynamics, which motivates a refined set of desiderata that we term maximal scale stability. Guided by this principle, we derive a Maximally Scale-Stable Parameterization (MSSP) for both SGD and Adam in all three scaling regimes, and characterize the corresponding limiting dynamics - qualitatively distinct from the $μ$P limit - through a separate DMFT analysis. Experiments verify that MSSP robustly recovers learning rate transfer and monotonic improvement with scale across regimes. Combined with existing depth-scaling theory, these results provide a complete scaling prescription for MoE architectures as a function of width, depth, expert width, and number of experts.

We propose a fine-grained CBM framework that grounds each concept in localized visual evidence, enabling direct inspection of where and how concepts are encoded. Experiments on medical imaging benchmarks show that our learned concept space is information-complete and achieves predictive performance comparable to standard CBMs, while substantially improving transparency. Unlike post-hoc attribution methods, our framework validates both the presence and correctness of concept representations, bridging interpretability with verifiability. ### [68] [PreFT: Prefill-only finetuning for efficient inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14217)
*Andrew Lanpouthakoun,Aryaman Arora,Zhengxuan Wu,Dhruv Pai,Ben Keigwin,Dan Jurafsky,Christopher Potts*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决大规模个性化LLM服务中多适配器带来的解码阶段吞吐瓶颈，本文提出PreFT（仅预填充微调），通过仅在预填充阶段使用适配器，实现了更高的吞吐效率，同时在RL任务中保持了与传统PEFT相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的参数高效微调（PEFT）在处理多用户个性化适配器时，由于解码阶段的计算特性，导致系统吞吐量大幅下降，难以满足大规模个性化服务的高效需求。

Method: 研究者提出PreFT方法，仅在预填充阶段（prefill）应用适配器，在生成阶段（decode）则丢弃适配器。作者在vLLM推理引擎上实现了针对LoRA和ReFT的PreFT优化版本，并通过增加适配器秩（rank）来补偿性能损失。

Result: 在Llama 3.1 70B模型上，当同时服务512个适配器时，PreFT相比传统PEFT吞吐量提升了1.9倍。在监督微调（SFT）任务中，虽然PreFT损失略高，但可通过提升秩来弥补且不影响吞吐量；在强化学习（RL）任务中，PreFT的表现与标准PEFT基本持平。

Conclusion: 本文验证了“仅预填充微调”（PreFT）是一种在大规模个性化LLM服务中，实现准确性与吞吐量之间更优权衡的方案。它打破了传统PEFT在多适配器服务中存在的解码阶段吞吐量瓶颈。

Abstract: Large language models can now be personalised efficiently at scale using parameter efficient finetuning methods (PEFTs), but serving user-specific PEFTs harms throughput, even with specialised kernels and memory management techniques. This is because, theoretically and empirically, a mismatch exists between prefill (processing a large number of tokens at once) and decode (generating a single token autoregressively): the latter has far lower throughput when serving multiple adapters. Rather than optimising performance relative to parameter count, for efficient multi-adapter serving, we instead ought to optimise performance relative to serving throughput. We therefore propose PreFT (Prefill-only Finetuning), wherein we only apply the adapter to prefill tokens and discard it afterwards. PreFT significantly increases throughput with minimal effect on performance. We develop and release an efficient implementation of two prefill-only PEFTs, LoRA and ReFT, on the vLLM inference engine. We first show that serving multi-user PreFTs is more efficient than traditional PEFTs ($1.9\times$ the throughput when serving $512$ adapters on Llama 3.1 70B). Then, we compare the performance of prefill-only vs. all-token adapters on a variety of supervised finetuning and reinforcement learning tasks with LMs at varying scales. On SFT, we observe that the evaluation loss of PreFTs is higher than PEFTs, but can be compensated by increasing rank with nearly no reduction in throughput. On RL, we consistently find that PreFTs approach parity with standard PEFTs. Together, this work validates prefill-only adaptation of LLMs as a more favourable accuracy-throughput tradeoff than existing PEFTs for personalised serving.

</details>


### [69] [Diagnosing Training Inference Mismatch in LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14220)
*Tianle Zhong,Neiwen Ling,Yifan Pi,Zijun Wei,Tianshu Yu,Geoffrey Fox,Peng Wu,Xiao Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了LLM强化学习中普遍存在的“训练-推理不匹配”（TIM）问题，证明了这种实现上的数值差异会导致训练崩溃，并呼吁将其视为影响系统稳定性的核心因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大语言模型（LLM）强化学习系统通常将采样（rollout）与策略优化过程分离。虽然两者逻辑上应使用相同的模型权重，但实现上的差异会导致对同一序列产生不同的概率预测，从而引发训练-推理不匹配（TIM），研究者旨在量化该现象对模型训练稳定性的影响。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为“VeXact”的零失配诊断设置，用于隔离并测量由数值实现差异导致的TIM现象，分析其对训练的影响，并识别出了一系列缓解TIM的补救措施。

Result: 研究表明，即使是微小的标记级数值不一致也足以导致训练崩溃；TIM改变了强化学习的有效优化目标，是导致LLM强化学习训练不稳定的主要原因之一。

Conclusion: 训练-推理不匹配（TIM）并非良性的数值噪声，而是导致LLM强化学习训练不稳定的关键系统性因素，必须在系统架构和算法层面予以重视并加以缓解。

Abstract: Modern LLM RL systems separate rollout generation from policy optimization. These two stages are expected to produce token probabilities that match exactly. However, implementation differences can make them assign different values to the same sequence under the same model weights, inducing Training-Inference Mismatch (TIM). TIM is difficult to inspect because it is entangled with off-policy drift and common stabilization mechanisms. In this work, we isolate TIM in a zero-mismatch diagnostic setting (VeXact), and show that small token-level numerical disagreements can independently cause training collapse. We further show that TIM changes the effective optimization problem, and identify a set of remedies that could mitigate TIM. Our results suggest that TIM is not benign numerical noise, but a systems-level perturbation that should be treated as a first-order factor in analyzing LLM RL stability.

</details>

This highlights the importance of leveraging large, multi-hospital health systems for training and validation to better reflect real-world clinical complexity. In this work, we develop DT-Transformer, a foundation model trained on 57.1M structured EHR entries over 1.7M patients from Mass General Brigham (MGB), spanning 11 hospitals and a broad network of outpatient clinics. DT-Transformer achieves strong discrimination in both held-out and prospective validation settings. Next-event prediction achieves a median age- and sex-stratified AUC of 0.871 across 896 disease categories, with all categories exceeding AUC 0.5. These results support health system-scale training as a path toward foundation models suited to real-world clinical forecasting.

### [71] [AudioMosaic: Contrastive Masked Audio Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14231)
*Hanxun Huang,Qizhou Wang,Xingjun Ma,Cihang Xie,Christopher Leckie,Sarah Erfani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AudioMosaic 是一种新型对比学习音频编码器，通过创新的时频掩码技术实现了高效预训练，在多项基准测试中性能领先，并具备强大的跨领域迁移与多模态集成能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管生成式自监督学习在音频领域取得了进展，但对比学习在音频中仍面临有效增强策略缺失和计算资源需求大等挑战。本文旨在通过改进对比学习策略，提升音频编码器学习判别性表征的能力及其在多场景下的迁移表现。

Method: 提出了一种基于对比学习的音频编码器 AudioMosaic。其核心创新在于采用“结构化时频掩码”（structured time-frequency masking）技术来构建正样本对，从而显著降低了内存消耗，支持高效的大批量（large-batch）预训练。

Result: 实验结果表明，AudioMosaic 在多个标准音频基准测试中在线性探测（linear probing）和微调（fine-tuning）设置下均达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能。此外，将其集成到音频-语言模型中可显著提升多模态任务的效果。

Conclusion: AudioMosaic 提供了一种高效且性能卓越的音频自监督学习框架。通过对比学习范式与创新的时频掩码策略，该模型不仅在通用音频理解任务上优于现有的生成式方法，还展现出极强的迁移能力，为音频-语言多模态研究提供了有力的基础架构。

Abstract: Audio self-supervised learning (SSL) aims to learn general-purpose representations from large-scale unlabeled audio data. While recent advances have been driven mainly by generative reconstruction objectives, contrastive approaches remain less explored, partly due to the difficulty of designing effective audio augmentations and the large batch sizes required for contrastive pre-training. We introduce \textbf{AudioMosaic}, a contrastive learning-based audio encoder for general audio understanding. During pre-training, AudioMosaic constructs positive pairs by applying structured time-frequency masking to spectrogram patches, which reduces memory usage and enables efficient large-batch training. Compared with generative approaches, the AudioMosaic encoder learns more discriminative utterance-level representations that demonstrate strong transferability across datasets, domains, and acoustic conditions. Extensive experiments show that AudioMosaic achieves state-of-the-art performance on several standard audio benchmarks under both linear probing and fine-tuning. We further show that integrating the pretrained AudioMosaic encoder into audio-language models improves performance on audio-language tasks. The code is publicly available in our \href{https://github.com/HanxunH/AudioMosaic}{GitHub repository}.

### [72] [Quantum Advantage in Multi Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14235)
*Simranjeet Singh Dahia,Claudia Szabo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过CHSH博弈和合作导航任务，证实了在QMARL中量子纠缠是突破经典性能上限的必要机制，并指出混合型架构是当前实现最佳协同效果的有效路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有QMARL研究普遍缺乏可证明的基准，导致难以严格区分所谓的“量子优势”是真正源于量子力学特性，还是仅仅由于算法偶然性。研究旨在通过科学实验验证量子纠缠在智能体协调中的核心作用，并量化其量子优势。

Method: 提出了一个去中心化的量子多智能体强化学习（QMARL）框架，采用变分量子电路（VQC）作为参与者，并通过共享纠缠态进行协同。利用CHSH博弈（具有明确的经典性能上限）作为基准，对比了纠缠量子策略、非纠缠量子策略与经典策略的性能差异；同时在合作导航任务（CoopNav）中评估了混合配置（量子参与者+经典集中式评论家）的有效性。

Result: 在CHSH博弈中，纠缠QMARL智能体达到了0.854的Tsirelson极限，远超0.75的经典上限；而非纠缠量子电路则维持在经典水平。在合作导航任务中，QMARL在不使用纠缠的情况下已实现约2倍于经典MAA2C的成功率，且结合量子参与者与经典评论家的混合模型取得了最佳综合性能。

Conclusion: 研究证明，在量子多智能体强化学习中，量子纠缠是实现超越经典性能极限的关键驱动力。混合型架构（量子参与者与经典集中式评论家）在复杂多智能体任务中表现出显著优势。此外，纠缠结构的合理选择对于性能提升至关重要，不当的纠缠反而会抑制协调效果。

Abstract: We present an empirical evaluation of quantum entanglement in agent coordination within quantum multi agent reinforcement learning (QMARL). While QMARL has attracted growing interest recently, most prior work evaluates quantum policies without provable baselines, making it impossible to rigorously distinguish quantum advantage from algorithmic coincidence. We address this directly by evaluating a decentralized QMARL framework with variational quantum circuit (VQC) actors with shared entangled states. In the CHSH game, which has a mathematically proven classical performance ceiling of 0.75 win rate, we show that entangled QMARL agents approach the Tsirelson limit of 0.854, providing clear evidence of their quantum advantage. We show that unentangled quantum circuits match the classical baseline, confirming that entanglement and not the quantum circuit itself is the active coordination mechanism. We also explore the effect of specific entanglement structures, as some Bell states enable coordination gains while others actively harm performance. On cooperative navigation (CoopNav), QMARL without entanglement achieves $\sim2\times$ improvement in success rate over classical MAA2C ($\sim$0.85 versus $\sim$0.40), with the hybrid configuration, quantum actor paired with a classical centralised critic, outperforming both fully classical and fully quantum solutions. We present our experimental analysis and discuss future work.

*Jeremías Figueiredo Paschmann,Juan Kaplan,Francisco Nattero Santiago Mauricio Barron Bucolo,Juan Wisznia,Luciano del Corro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将两两排序提示（PRP）转化为主动学习的排序方法，通过主动排序器和随机化方向预言机，在有限的调用预算下有效解决了LLM判断中的噪声和位置偏差问题，提高了排序精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于两两排序提示（PRP）的方法通常依赖传统排序算法，但由于LLM生成的判断存在噪声、顺序敏感性及传递性失效等问题，导致在调用预算受限时无法获取可靠的前K个排序结果。

Method: 将PRP重构为主动学习框架，利用主动排序器（active rankers）替代传统排序算法，并引入了“随机方向预言机（randomized-direction oracle）”，通过在单次调用中引入零均值噪声来消除位置偏差。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在调用受限的场景下显著提升了NDCG@10指标，且通过随机化方向预言机实现了无偏差的聚合排序，无需额外的双向调用成本。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，将两两排序提示（PRP）重构为带噪两两比较的主动学习问题，可以有效提升在有限调用预算下的排序效果，并提供了一种通过随机化方向预言机消除系统性位置偏差的鲁棒方案。

Abstract: Pairwise Ranking Prompting (PRP) elicits pairwise preference judgments from an LLM, which are then aggregated into a ranking, usually via classical sorting algorithms. However, judgments are noisy, order-sensitive, and sometimes intransitive, so sorting assumptions do not match the setting. Because sorting aims to recover a full permutation, truncating it to meet a call budget does not produce a dependable top-K. We thus reframe PRP reranking as active learning from noisy pairwise comparisons and show that active rankers are drop-in replacements that improve NDCG@10 per call in the call-constrained regime. Our noise-robust framework also introduces a randomized-direction oracle that uses a single LLM call per pair. This approach converts systematic position bias into zero-mean noise, enabling unbiased aggregate ranking without the cost of bidirectional calls.

### [74] [Paraphrasing Attack Resilience of Various AI-Generated Text Detection Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14240)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）的普及，剽窃和虚假信息传播等问题日益严重，且避开AI检测的工具不断涌现，开发可靠的机器生成文本检测技术变得迫切，因此需要评估现有检测方法对改写攻击的防御能力。

Method: 研究评估了三种主要的机器生成文本检测方法：微调后的RoBERTa模型、Binoculars算法以及基于文本特征的分析方法，并利用随机森林分类器对上述方法进行集成，通过模拟改写攻击（Paraphrasing attacks）来测试各方法的鲁棒性。

Result: 研究发现，包含Binoculars算法的集成模型在初始性能上表现最强，但在遭遇改写攻击时，其性能下降最为显著。整体而言，没有一种现有方法能在高检测准确率和高攻击鲁棒性之间取得完美平衡。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了AI文本检测领域存在“性能”与“鲁棒性”之间的二分法（Dichotomy），即表现最优的检测模型往往在面对改写攻击时性能下降最明显，这挑战了当前对现有检测技术可靠性的认知。

Abstract: The recent large-scale emergence of LLMs has left an open space for dealing with their consequences, such as plagiarism or the spread of false information on the Internet. Coupling this with the rise of AI detector bypassing tools, reliable machine-generated text detection is in increasingly high demand. We investigate the paraphrasing attack resilience of various machine-generated text detection methods, evaluating three approaches: fine-tuned RoBERTa, Binoculars, and text feature analysis, along with their ensembles using Random Forest classifiers. We discovered that Binoculars-inclusive ensembles yield the strongest results, but they also suffer the most significant losses during attacks. In this paper, we present the dichotomy of performance versus resilience in the world of AI text detection, which complicates the current perception of reliability among state-of-the-art techniques.

### [75] [Latency-Quality Routing for Functionally Equivalent Tools in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14241)
*Kexin Chu,Dawei Xiang,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 LLM 工具调用中多个同类提供商的路由难题，本文提出了 LQM-ContextRoute 算法。该算法通过将延迟视为服务容量而非简单的惩罚项，并结合在线反馈学习，实现了在保证响应质量的同时优化延迟，显著优于传统的 SW-UCB 方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着工具增强型大语言模型（LLM）的发展，智能体往往需要面对多个功能等价的提供商。在面临运行时负载时，现有的路由策略难以在延迟、可靠性和响应质量之间取得平衡，特别是在缺乏金标准（Gold Labels）的情况下，传统的加性奖励机制容易导致性能崩塌。

Method: 提出了一种名为 LQM-ContextRoute 的上下文多臂老虎机（Contextual Bandit）路由算法。其核心设计是“延迟-质量匹配”（Latency-Quality Matching），通过将延迟视为服务容量来对提供商进行排序，结合特定查询的质量估计以及 LLM-as-a-judge 的在线反馈机制，实现对提供商性能的动态适应。

Result: 在 web-search 任务中，F1 分数比 SW-UCB 提升了 2.18 个百分点；在高异构性的 StrategyQA 设置中，准确率提升高达 18 个百分点；在异构检索器池中，NDCG 指标提升了 2.91 到 3.22 个百分点。该方法成功在提升质量的同时保持了优异的延迟表现。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，在工具调用路由中，将延迟视为服务容量（而非仅作为奖励函数的负面惩罚项）是解决多提供商负载均衡问题的关键。LQM-ContextRoute 通过有效处理提供商的质量异构性和运行时负载压力，显著提升了工具使用效果。

Abstract: Tool-augmented LLM agents increasingly access the same tool type through multiple functionally equivalent providers, such as web-search APIs, retrievers, or LLM backends exposed behind a shared interface. This creates a provider-routing problem under runtime load: the router must choose among providers that differ in latency, reliability, and answer quality, often without gold labels at deployment time. We introduce LQM-ContextRoute, a contextual bandit router for same-function tool providers. Its key design is latency-quality matching: instead of letting low latency offset poor answers in an additive reward, the router ranks providers by expected answer quality per service cycle. It combines this capacity-aware score with query-specific quality estimation and LLM-as-judge feedback, allowing it to adapt online to both load changes and provider-quality differences. On the main web-search load benchmark, LQM-ContextRoute improves F1 by +2.18 pp over SW-UCB while staying on the latency-quality frontier. In a high-heterogeneity StrategyQA setting, LQM-ContextRoute avoids additive-reward collapse and improves accuracy by up to +18 pp over SW-UCB; on heterogeneous retriever pools, it improves NDCG by +2.91--+3.22 pp over SW-UCB. These results show that same-function tool routing benefits from treating latency as service capacity, especially when runtime pressure and provider-quality heterogeneity coexist.

### [77] [Architecture-Aware Explanation Auditing for Industrial Visual Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14255)
*Sibo Jia,Zihang Zhao,Kunrong Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文针对工业视觉检测中深度学习模型解释不可靠的问题，提出了一种“架构感知解释审计协议”。研究发现，解释的忠实度取决于模型结构与解释器的匹配程度（原生读出机制），建议未来应将解释路径与模型架构协同设计，并配套定量评估指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在工业视觉检测中，虽然深度分类器的热力图解释看起来合理，但往往无法准确反映模型的实际决策依据。现有的解释方法缺乏标准化的审计流程，导致难以量化评估解释的忠实度，因此迫切需要一种能够评估解释方法与模型决策机制兼容性的方法。

Method: 作者建立了一个“架构感知解释审计协议”，基于“原生读出假设”（即解释方法的忠实度受限于其与模型原生决策机制的结构距离）。通过在WM-811K晶圆图数据集上，使用三种不同种子下的零填充扰动协议，对比了ViT、Swin、ResNet、DenseNet等架构结合不同解释方法（Attention Rollout, Grad-CAM, RISE）的删除AUC（Deletion AUC），并进行了模糊填充灵敏度分析及MVTec AD数据集的边界条件探索。

Result: 研究发现：1. 读出结构（而非单纯的架构族）决定了解释的兼容性；2. 在WM-811K任务中，ViT-Tiny + Attention Rollout表现出显著优于其他方法的删除AUC（0.211）；3. 模型无关的方法（RISE）在某些情况下优于原生方法，证明原生读出是兼容性原则而非最优保证；4. 解释的忠实度排名高度依赖于扰动基线和数据集，具有任务特异性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了解释的可信度并非模型架构本身决定的，而是由模型、解释器与扰动算子共同构成。通过引入“原生读出机制”这一核心概念，作者提出解释路径应与模型架构进行协同设计，并强调在部署视觉检测系统时，必须辅以定量的忠实度指标。

Abstract: Industrial visual inspection systems increasingly rely on deep classifiers whose heatmap explanations may appear visually plausible while failing to identify the image regions that actually drive model decisions. This paper operationalizes an architecture-aware explanation audit protocol grounded in the native-readout hypothesis: the perturbation-based faithfulness of an explanation method is bounded by its structural distance from the model's native decision mechanism. On WM-811K wafer maps (9 classes, 172k images) under a three-seed zero-fill perturbation protocol, ViT-Tiny + Attention Rollout attains Deletion AUC 0.211 against 0.432-0.525 for Swin-Tiny / ResNet18+CBAM / DenseNet121 + Grad-CAM (abs(Cohen's d) > 1.1), despite lower classification accuracy. Swin-Tiny disentangles architecture family from readout structure: despite being a Transformer, its spatial feature-map hierarchy makes it Grad-CAM compatible, showing that the operative factor is readout structure rather than architecture family. A model-agnostic control (RISE) compresses all families to Deletion AUC about 0.1, indicating the gap arises from the explainer pathway; notably, RISE outperforms all native methods, so native readout is a compatibility principle rather than an optimality guarantee. A blur-fill sensitivity analysis shows that the family ordering reverses under a different perturbation baseline, reinforcing that faithfulness rankings are joint properties of (model, explainer, perturbation operator) triples. An exploratory boundary-condition study on MVTec AD (pretrained models) indicates that audit results are dataset/task dependent and identifies conditions requiring qualification. The protocol yields actionable guidance: explanation pathways should be co-designed with model architectures based on readout structure, and deployed heatmaps should be accompanied by quantitative faithfulness metrics.

</details>


### [78] [TILT: Target-induced loss tilting under covariate shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14280)
*Kakei Yamamoto,Martin J. Wainwright*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TILT 是一种处理无监督领域适应的新框架，它通过在目标域惩罚预测器的辅助分量，无需显式密度比估计即可实现鲁棒的跨域泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无监督领域适应（UDA）中，处理协变量偏移（covariate shift）时，传统的重要性加权方法在源域和目标域支持集不相交或分布差异极大时往往失效或不稳定。因此，需要一种更稳健、无需显式估计密度比的自适应方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“目标诱导损失倾斜（TILT）”的新颖目标函数。该方法将源预测器分解为 $f+b$ 两部分，在有标签的源数据上优化总函数，同时在无标签的目标数据上对辅助项 $b$ 进行惩罚。最终仅部署 $f$ 作为目标预测器，通过这种机制在人口层面隐式地诱导权重分配。

Result: 理论上，证明了 TILT 产生的估计量在源-目标对存在支持集不相交的情况下仍能保持一致有界，并给出了有限样本下的预言机不等式。在回归问题和 CIFAR-100 蒸馏实验中，TILT 的性能优于源域训练、精确重要性加权及相对密度比基准。

Conclusion: TILT 提供了一种在无监督领域适应中处理协变量偏移的有效且稳定的方法。它通过辅助项的惩罚机制，不仅在理论上克服了传统重要性加权方法在支持集不相交时的局限性，还在实践中表现出比现有基准方法更强的鲁棒性和性能。

Abstract: We introduce and analyze Target-Induced Loss Tilting (TILT) for unsupervised domain adaptation under covariate shift. It is based on a novel objective function that decomposes the source predictor as $f+b$, fits $f+b$ on labeled source data while simultaneously penalizing the auxiliary component $b$ on unlabeled target inputs. The resulting fit $f$ is deployed as the final target predictor. At the population level, we show that this target-side penalty implicitly induces relative importance weighting at the population level, but in terms of an estimand $b^*_f$ that is self-localized to the current error, and remains uniformly bounded for any source-target pair (even those with disjoint supports). We prove a general finite-sample oracle inequality on the excess risk, and use it to give an end-to-end guarantee for training with sparse ReLU networks. Experiments on controlled regression problems and shifted CIFAR-100 distillation show that TILT improves target-domain performance over source-only training, exact importance weighting, and relative density-ratio baselines, with a stable dependence on the regularization parameter.

</details>


### [79] [Minimal-Intervention KV Retention: A Design-Space Study and a Diversity-Penalty Survivor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14292)
*Libo Sun,Po-wei Harn,Peixiong He,Xiao Qin*

Method: 研究者首先评估了七种现有的KV缓存压缩机制，并指出其在数学推理任务中表现不佳。随后提出了一种名为“α”的改进方案，该方案通过修改TriAttention的评分函数，用基于设施选址启发式的贪婪选择算法替换了传统的argmax-top-k，并引入了一个由权重λ控制的V空间冗余惩罚项。

Conclusion: 针对极低KV缓存预算下的模型推理，通过修改注意力评分机制（引入V空间冗余惩罚的贪婪选择策略）比复杂的结构性重构更有效。此外，采用严格的验证协议（预注册、独立测试集、符号评估）对于科学评估压缩算法的真实有效性至关重要。

Abstract: KV-cache compression at small budgets is a crowded design space spanning cache representation, head-wise routing, compression cadence, decoding behavior, and within-budget scoring. We study seven mechanisms across these five families under matched mean cache on long-form mathematical reasoning (MATH-500~\cite{hendrycks2021math}) with two distilled-reasoning models (Qwen-7B and Llama-8B variants of DeepSeek-R1-Distill~\cite{deepseek2025r1}) at budgets $b \in \{64, 128\}$. All seven were rejected. We then propose $α$, a one-function modification to the TriAttention~\cite{mao2026triattention} retention scorer that replaces argmax-top-$k$ with greedy facility-location-inspired selection under a V-space redundancy penalty controlled by a single weight $λ$. A pre-registered protocol tunes $λ$ on a frozen development split and confirms on a disjoint held-out split; with $λ= 0.5$, $α$ clears Bonferroni on two of the four (model, budget) cells (Qwen $b{=}128$ and Llama $b{=}64$), no cell is significantly negative, and the pre-registered Branch~A triggers. The finding is asymmetric: a minimal scoring modification beat heavier structural redesigns in this regime, and the combined matched-memory, sympy-graded, held-out confirmation protocol is the evidence standard that made the asymmetry visible.

### [80] [Policy Optimization in Hybrid Discrete-Continuous Action Spaces via Mixed Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14297)
*Matias Alvo,Daniel Russo,Yash Kanoria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对混合离散-连续动作空间的强化学习难题，提出了“混合策略优化（HPO）”，通过融合路径导数与得分函数，实现了在保持梯度无偏性的同时大幅提升学习效率和稳定性，有效解决了高维空间中的梯度质量问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人、控制及运筹等领域中，混合离散-连续动作空间问题十分常见。现有的无模型策略梯度方法（基于得分函数）在高维空间中面临严重的信度分配问题，而现有的可微仿真方法在处理离散动作或非平滑动力学时，往往会导致梯度偏倚或信息缺失。为了解决这些限制，研究者旨在开发一种能高效利用仿真器导数信息并兼顾离散决策的优化策略。

Method: 作者提出了“混合策略优化”（Hybrid Policy Optimization, HPO）。该方法利用可微仿真（differentiable simulation）技术，在平滑区域进行路径求导（pathwise gradients），在非平滑或离散区域结合得分函数（score-function）估计器，构建了一种保持无偏性的混合梯度估计方法。同时，通过将动作不连续问题重构为混合形式以扩展适用范围。

Result: 实验结果表明，在库存控制和切换线性二次调节器（switched LQR）问题中，HPO 的表现显著优于 PPO。随着连续动作空间维度的增加，HPO 的性能优势愈发明显。此外，理论分析证明了混合梯度在接近最优策略时的方差缩减特性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入混合梯度估计器，有效结合了路径导数与得分函数，为混合离散-连续动作空间提供了一种高效、无偏且鲁棒的优化方案。理论分析表明，在接近最优解时，该方法的交叉项影响可忽略不计，从而支持离散与连续组件的近似解耦优化。

Abstract: We study reinforcement learning in hybrid discrete-continuous action spaces, such as settings where the discrete component selects a regime (or index) and the continuous component optimizes within it -- a structure common in robotics, control, and operations problems. Standard model-free policy gradient methods rely on score-function (SF) estimators and suffer from severe credit-assignment issues in high-dimensional settings, leading to poor gradient quality. On the other hand, differentiable simulation largely sidesteps these issues by backpropagating through a simulator, but the presence of discrete actions or non-smooth dynamics yields biased or uninformative gradients. To address this, we propose Hybrid Policy Optimization (HPO), which backpropagates through the simulator wherever smoothness permits, using a mixed gradient estimator that combines pathwise and SF gradients while maintaining unbiasedness. We also show how problems with action discontinuities can be reformulated in hybrid form, further broadening its applicability. Empirically, HPO substantially outperforms PPO on inventory control and switched linear-quadratic regulator problems, with performance gaps increasing as the continuous action dimension grows. Finally, we characterize the structure of the mixed gradient, showing that its cross term -- which captures how continuous actions influence future discrete decisions -- becomes negligible near a discrete best response, thereby enabling approximate decentralized updates of the continuous and discrete components and reducing variance near optimality. All resources are available at github.com/MatiasAlvo/hybrid-rl.

Method: 提出了一种语言诱导先验（LIP）框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）处理目标域的专家文本描述，将其转化为选择模型。该模型被整合进期望最大化（EM）算法中，用以评估源域的相关性；在目标数据稀缺时依靠LIP引导源域选择，随着数据增加自动优化选择结果。

Result: 实验表明，该框架在描述性（高斯估计）、预测性（C-MAPSS数据集）和规定性（MuJoCo hopper）任务中均表现优异；理论证明显示，该估计器在先验正确时接近神谕（oracle）水平，且无论先验质量如何，均保持渐进一致性。

Abstract: Domain adaptation faces a fundamental paradox in the cold-start regime. When target data is scarce, statistical methods fail to distinguish relevant source domains from irrelevant ones, which often leads to negative transfer. In this paper, we address this challenge by leveraging expert textual descriptions of the target domain, a resource that is often available but overlooked. We propose a probabilistic framework that translates these semantic descriptions into a choice model, namely a Language-Induced Prior (LIP), that learns the preferences from a pretrained Large Language Model (LLM). The LIP is then integrated into an Expectation-Maximization algorithm to identify source relevance. Methodologically, this framework is compatible with any parametric model where a likelihood is available. It allows the LIP to guide the selection of sources when target signals are weak, while gradually refining these choices as samples accumulate. Theoretically, we prove that the estimator roughly matches an oracle cold-start MSE under a correct prior, while remaining asymptotically consistent regardless of the quality of the LIP. Empirically, we validated the framework on a descriptive (Gaussian estimation), a predictive (C-MAPSS dataset), and a prescriptive task (MuJoCo hopper).

### [82] [Matrix-Space Reinforcement Learning for Reusing Local Transition Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14304)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Compositional generalization in sequential decision-making requires identifying which parts of prior rollouts remain useful for new tasks. Existing methods reuse skills or predictive models, but often overlook rich local transition geometry and dynamics. We propose Matrix-Space Reinforcement Learning (MSRL), a geometric abstraction that represents trajectory segments through positive semidefinite matrix descriptors aggregating first- and second-order statistics of lifted one-step transitions. These descriptors expose shared hidden structure, support algebraic composition in an abstract matrix space, and reveal opportunities for transfer. We prove that the descriptor is well defined up to coordinate gauge, complete for the induced low-order additive signal class, additive under valid segment composition, and minimally sufficient among admissible additive descriptors. We further show that conditioning value functions on the trajectory-segment matrix yields a first-order smooth approximation of action values, enabling source-learned matrix-to-value mappings to bootstrap learning in new tasks. MSRL is plug-in compatible with standard model-free and model-based methods, while obstruction filtering rejects implausible compositions. ### [83] [Beyond Binary: Reframing GUI Critique as Continuous Semantic Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14311)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GUI智能体测试时扩展（TTS）依赖于二分类判别模型（Critic），但这种方法存在“可供性坍塌”（Affordance Collapse）和对噪声敏感的问题，导致模型无法区分有效操作与看似合理但无效的干扰项。

Method: 提出了BBCritic（Beyond-Binary Critic），基于功能等价假设（Functional Equivalence Hypothesis），通过两阶段对比学习将指令与操作对齐到共享的“可供性空间”（Affordance Space），从而恢复层次化结构；同时构建了BBBench评价基准，通过四级分类法对密集动作空间进行精细化评估。

Conclusion: GUI评价任务本质上是一个度量学习（Metric Learning）问题，而非简单的二分类问题。引入层次化的评价机制能有效提升GUI智能体的推理和排序能力。

Abstract: Test-Time Scaling (TTS), which samples multiple candidate actions and ranks them via a Critic Model, has emerged as a promising paradigm for generalist GUI agents. Its efficacy thus hinges on the critic's fine-grained ranking ability. However, existing GUI critic models uniformly adopt binary classification. Our motivational analysis of these models exposes a severe entanglement: scores for valid actions and plausible-but-invalid distractors become indistinguishable. We attribute this failure to two structural defects: Affordance Collapse--the hierarchical affordance space is compressed into 0/1 labels; and Noise Sensitivity--binary objectives overfit to noisy decision boundaries. To resolve this, we introduce BBCritic (Beyond-Binary Critic), a paradigm shift grounded in the Functional Equivalence Hypothesis. Through two-stage contrastive learning, BBCritic aligns instructions and actions in a shared Affordance Space, recovering the hierarchical structure that binary supervision flattens. We also present BBBench (Beyond-Binary Bench), the first GUI critic benchmark that pairs a dense action space with a hierarchical four-level taxonomy, enabling fine-grained ranking evaluation. Experimental results show that BBCritic-3B, trained without any extra annotation, outperforms 7B-parameter SOTA binary models. It demonstrates strong zero-shot transferability across platforms and tasks, supporting our methodological view: GUI critique is fundamentally a metric-learning problem, not a classification one.

### [84] [Guided Diffusion Sampling for Precipitation Forecast Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14317)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于扩散采样的梯度引导框架。该方法不直接扰动大气状态，而是通过在扩散模型采样过程中引入引导机制，在保持大气分布一致性的前提下，导航采样轨迹以实现降水量的减少。

Abstract: Extreme precipitation causes severe societal and economic damage, and weather control has long been discussed as a potential mitigation strategy. However, to the best of our knowledge, perturbation-based interventions for weather control using data-driven weather forecasting models have not yet been explored. While adversarial attacks also generate perturbations that alter forecasts, they aim to exploit model artifacts and do not account for physical plausibility. In this paper, we propose a gradient-based guidance framework for precipitation-reduction interventions through diffusion sampling in diffusion-based weather forecasting models. Instead of directly perturbing atmospheric states, our method steers the diffusion sampling trajectory, enabling precipitation reduction while maintaining consistency with the atmospheric distribution. To assess physical plausibility, we evaluate from three perspectives: (i) vertical and variable-wise perturbation profiles, (ii) latent-space trajectory deviation, and (iii) cross-model transferability. Experiments on extreme precipitation events from WeatherBench2 demonstrate that our method achieves effective precipitation reduction while yielding more physically plausible interventions than adversarial perturbations.
