### [87] [Nearest-Neighbor Radii under Dependent Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14343)
*Yuanyuan Gao,Yilong Hou,Zhexiao Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了依赖采样下最近邻半径的几何特性，证明了即使在存在数据依赖性的情况下，最近邻方法依然适用，并提出了不依赖环境维数、仅取决于局部固有维数的非渐近误差界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的最近邻方法主要基于独立同分布（i.i.d.）数据的几何特性分析。然而，在许多实际应用（如时间序列分析）中，数据往往存在时间或空间上的相关性。本文旨在探究数据依赖性是否会从根本上改变最近邻邻域的尺度，并为处理非独立高维数据提供理论支持。

Method: 本文采用了概率论中的强混合（strong mixing）假设来建模数据的依赖性。通过分析多项式混合下的几乎处处收敛性，以及几何混合下的尖锐非渐近矩界，研究了依赖采样下最近邻半径的分布特性。此外，通过引入局部固有维数（local intrinsic dimension）来刻画数据的几何结构，从而避免了“维度灾难”。

Result: 实验结果显示，所提出的理论在合成数据及真实世界的时间序列基准测试中均得到了验证。研究表明，即便在存在依赖性的采样条件下，最近邻几何结构依然能提供有效的信息，且该方法对于集中在低维流形上的高维数据具有良好的适应性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，即使在数据存在依赖性的情况下，最近邻半径的几何特性依然保持有效。本文建立的理论框架不仅证明了其渐近收敛性，还揭示了非渐近矩界与局部固有维数（而非环境维数）之间的关系，验证了最近邻方法在复杂依赖数据（如时间序列）中的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Nearest-neighbor methods are fundamental to classical and modern machine learning, yet their geometric properties are typically analyzed under independent sampling. In this paper, we study the nearest-neighbor radii under dependent sampling. We consider strong mixing dependent observations and ask whether dependence changes the scale of nearest-neighbor neighborhoods. We establish distribution-free almost sure convergence under polynomial mixing and sharp non-asymptotic moment bounds under geometric mixing. The moment bounds depend on the local intrinsic dimension rather than the ambient dimension, making the results applicable to high-dimensional data concentrated near lower-dimensional manifolds. Synthetic experiments and real-world time-series benchmarks support the theory, showing that nearest-neighbor geometry remains informative under dependence sampling.

### [88] [Exemplar Partitioning for Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14347)
*Jessica Rumbelow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“示例分区”（EP）的轻量级可解释性方法，通过基于样本的Voronoi划分构建特征字典，在计算成本降低1000倍的情况下，实现了与稀疏自编码器（SAE）相当甚至在某些指标上更优的特征解析与干预效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稀疏自编码器（SAE）方法在构建特征字典时计算开销巨大（需要大量训练Token），且不同模型、层或检查点之间的特征难以直接对齐和比较。为了解决这些问题，作者旨在提出一种更轻量、具备跨模型可比性且无需预设字典规模的可解释性方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“示例分区”（Exemplar Partitioning, EP）的无监督方法。该方法将激活空间视为Voronoi分区，通过对流式激活进行基于距离阈值的领导者聚类（Leader-Clustering）来构建字典。每个区域由一个具体的观察样本（Exemplar）作为锚点，既作为归属标准也作为干预方向，且字典规模由数据几何形状自适应决定。

Result: 在Gemma-2-2B模型上的实验表明：1. EP具有极高的构建效率（计算量比SAE少约1000倍）；2. EP区域具有可解释性且支持因果干预，能够有效抑制模型拒绝行为；3. 支持跨检查点对齐，能有效区分预训练与微调带来的特征差异；4. 在AxBench基准测试中，EP的平均AUROC达到0.881，表现优于基准SAE；5. EP还提供了天然的分布外（OOD）检测信号。

Conclusion: Exemplar Partitioning (EP) 是一种高效、可解释且易于跨模型比较的特征字典构建方法。它通过基于样本聚类的Voronoi划分，在极低的计算成本下实现了与稀疏自编码器（SAE）相当的特征提取和因果干预能力，为大规模语言模型的可解释性分析提供了更灵活的工具。

Abstract: We introduce Exemplar Partitioning (EP), an unsupervised method for constructing interpretable feature dictionaries from large language model activations with $\sim 10^{3}\times$ fewer tokens than comparable sparse autoencoders (SAEs). An EP dictionary is a Voronoi partition of activation space, built by leader-clustering streamed activations within a distance threshold. Each region is anchored by an observed exemplar that serves as both its membership criterion and intervention direction; dictionary size is not prespecified, but determined by the activation geometry at that threshold. Because exemplars are observed rather than learned, dictionaries built from the same data stream are directly comparable across layers, models, and training checkpoints.
  We characterise EP as an interpretability object via targeted demonstrations of properties newly accessible through this construction, plus one head-to-head benchmark. In Gemma-2-2B, EP dictionary regions are interpretable and support causal interventions: refusal in instruction-tuned Gemma concentrates in a region whose exemplar ablation can collapse held-out refusal. Cross-checkpoint matching between base and instruction-tuned dictionaries separates the directions preserved through finetuning from those introduced by it. EP regions and Gemma Scope SAE features decompose activation space differently but agree on a shared core: $\sim 20\%$ of EP regions match an SAE feature at $F_{1} > 0.5$, and EP one-hot probes retain $\sim 97\%$ of raw-activation probe accuracy at $\ell_{0} = 1$. Nearest-exemplar distance provides a free out-of-distribution signal at inference. On AxBench latent concept detection at Gemma-2-2B-it L20, EP at $p_{1}$ reaches mean AUROC $0.881$, $+0.126$ over the canonical GemmaScope SAE leaderboard entry and within $0.030$ of SAE-A's $0.911$, at $\sim 10^{3}\times$ less build compute.

### [89] [Distributionally Robust Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning via Adaptive Task Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14350)
*Nicholas E. Corrado,Wenyuan Huang,Josiah P. Hanna*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多任务强化学习中因数据分配不均导致的学习效率低下问题，本文提出了一种名为 DRATS 的自适应采样算法，通过优先分配资源给难以解决的任务，显著提升了多任务系统的整体性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多任务强化学习（MTRL）通常对所有任务分配相等的数据资源，导致“简单任务过剩、困难任务不足”的资源分配不均问题，进而引发学习效率低和任务间学习进度失衡。研究旨在解决这一因数据分配不均导致的性能瓶颈。

Method: 提出了一种名为“分布鲁棒自适应任务采样”（DRATS）的算法。该算法将多任务强化学习形式化为一个可行性问题，并推导出了一个极大极小（minimax）目标函数，旨在最小化各任务期望回报与实际回报之间的差距（return gap），从而实现对那些最难的任务进行优先采样。

Result: 在 MetaWorld-MT10 和 MT50 等基准测试中，DRATS 表现出优于现有任务采样算法的性能，显著提高了数据效率并提升了模型对困难任务的处理能力。

Conclusion: DRATS 算法通过动态调整任务采样策略，有效缓解了多任务强化学习中的数据分配不均衡问题，在提升数据利用效率和改善最差任务表现方面展现出显著优势。

Abstract: Multi-task reinforcement learning (MTRL) aims to train a single agent to efficiently optimize performance across multiple tasks simultaneously. However, jointly optimizing all tasks often yields imbalanced learning: agents quickly solve easy tasks but learn slowly on harder ones. While prior work primarily attributes this imbalance to conflicting task gradients and proposes gradient manipulation or specialized architectures to address it, we instead focus on a distinct and under-explored challenge: imbalanced data allocation. Standard MTRL allocates an equal number of environment interactions to each task, which over-allocates data to easy tasks that require relatively few interactions to solve and under-allocates data to hard tasks that require substantially more experience to solve. To address this challenge, we introduce Distributionally Robust Adaptive Task Sampling (DRATS), an algorithm that adaptively prioritizes sampling tasks furthest from being solved. We derive DRATS by formalizing MTRL as a feasibility problem from which we derive a minimax objective for minimizing the worst-case return gap, the difference between a desired target return and the agent's return on a task. In benchmarks like MetaWorld-MT10 and MT50, DRATS improves data efficiency and increases worst-task performance compared to existing task sampling algorithms.

Abstract: Vector quantization is a fundamental tool for compressing high-dimensional embeddings, yet existing multi-codebook methods rely on static codebooks that limit expressiveness under heterogeneous data geometry. We propose Residual Quantization via Mixture of Experts (RQ-MoE), a framework combining a two-level MoE with dual-stream quantization to enable input-dependent codebook adaptation for efficient vector quantization. RQ-MoE enables dynamic codebook construction and decouples instruction from quantization, facilitating parallel decoding. ### [91] [MoRe: Modular Representations for Principled Continual Representation Learning on Squantial Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14364)
*Jiaqi Sun,Boyang Sun,Mohamad Rasmy,Xiangchen Song,Kun Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的持续学习方法多侧重于修改参数或架构，缺乏对数据本质结构（而非任务边界）的有效利用；作者旨在解决持续学习中的核心矛盾——即如何在不干扰已有知识的前提下，通过识别并更新结构化的表征来实现对新信息的适应。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MoRe 的框架，旨在通过时间延迟依赖关系从数据中自动识别表征的模块化结构；该方法将知识解构为基础模块和特定模块的层级体系，通过可识别性保证实现模块的重用、对齐与扩展，在适应新任务的同时通过架构设计天然保留旧模块。

Result: 在合成数据集和真实大语言模型（LLM）激活上的实验结果表明，MoRe 能够提取出具有可解释性的层级结构，显著提升了模型在持续学习中的可塑性与稳定性权衡（plasticity-stability trade-offs）。

Conclusion: MoRe 通过在表征层面引入模块化，而非依赖传统的架构级分配，为持续学习提供了一种具有可解释性且能够有效平衡可塑性与稳定性的新范式，证明了基于数据固有结构的层级化表征是实现持续适应的关键。

Abstract: Continual learning requires models to adapt to new data while preserving previously acquired knowledge. At its core, this challenge can be viewed as principled one-step adaptation: incorporating new information with minimal interference to existing representations. Most existing approaches address this challenge by modifying model parameters or architectures in a supervised, task-specific manner. However, the underlying issue is representational: tasks require distinct yet structured representations that can be selectively updated without disrupting representations, while structure should reflect intrinsic organization in the data rather than task boundaries. In sequential data, time-delayed dependencies provide a natural signal for uncovering this organization, revealing how fundamental representations give rise to more specific ones. Inspired by the modular organization of the human brain, we propose MoRe, a framework that identifies modularity in the representation itself rather than allocating it at the architectural level. MoRe decomposes knowledge into a hierarchy of fundamental and specific modules with identifiability guarantees, enabling principled module reuse, alignment, and expansion during adaptation while preserving old modules by construction. Experiments on synthetic benchmarks and real-world LLM activations demonstrate interpretable hierarchical structure, improved plasticity-stability trade-offs, suggesting MoRe as a principled foundation for continual adaptation

### [92] [LoMETab: Beyond Rank-1 Ensembles for Tabular Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14365)
*Changryeol Choi,Hyewon Park,Yujin Kwon,Gowun Jeong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 LoMETab，一种基于低秩因子分解的隐式集成方法，通过参数化控制成员权重，实现了对表格模型预测多样性的灵活调节，打破了传统秩-1 集成架构的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前表格学习基准测试中领先模型表现趋同，亟需深入理解并控制提升简单神经表格模型竞争力的核心机制（如隐式集成），并克服现有秩-1 方法表达能力的限制。

Method: 提出 LoMETab 方法，通过将成员权重参数化为 $W_k = W \odot (1 + A_kB_k^\top)$，将传统的秩-1 BatchEnsemble/TabM 推广至秩-$r$ 的恒等残差哈达玛族（identity-residual Hadamard family），从而实现对模型多样性的显式控制。

Result: 理论上证明了当 $r \ge 2$ 时，该方法严格扩大了假设空间；实验表明 LoMETab 能够通过调整 $r$ 和 $\sigma_{\mathrm{init}}$ 实现对预测多样性（如 KL 散度、预测分歧等）的精确控制，且预测性能随数据集表现出依赖于这两个参数的网格特征。

Conclusion: LoMETab 不仅仅是一个固定的集成架构，而是一个可以通过调整低秩因子秩（rank）和初始化尺度（scale）来实现多样性可控的表格学习模型家族，为理解和优化神经表格模型提供了更灵活的框架。

Abstract: Recent tabular learning benchmarks increasingly show a tight performance cluster rather than a clear hierarchy among leading methods, spanning gradient boosted decision trees, attention-based architectures, and implicit ensembles such as TabM. As benchmark gains plateau, a complementary goal is to understand and control the mechanisms that make simple neural tabular models competitive. We propose LoMETab, a rank-$r$ generalization of multiplicative implicit ensembles. LoMETab lifts the rank-1 BatchEnsemble/TabM modulation to a rank-$r$ identity-residual Hadamard family by parameterizing each member weight as $W_k = W \odot (1 + A_kB_k^\top)$, where $W$ is shared and $(A_k, B_k)$ are member-specific low-rank factors. This exposes two practical diversity-control axes: the adapter rank $r$ and the initialization scale $σ_{\mathrm{init}}$, and we prove that for $r \ge 2$ this generalization strictly enlarges BatchEnsemble's hypothesis class. Empirically, we show that this added capacity manifests as measurable predictive diversity after training: on representative classification datasets, LoMETab sustains higher pairwise KL than an additive low-rank ablation, and $(r, σ_{\mathrm{init}})$ provides broad control over pairwise KL, varying by up to several orders of magnitude across configurations. The induced diversity is reflected in task-appropriate output-level measures: argmax disagreement for classification and ambiguity for regression, indicating that the control extends beyond pairwise KL to decision- and output-level member variation. Finally, experiments sweeping over adapter rank $r$ and initialization scale $σ_{\mathrm{init}}$ reveal that predictive performance is dataset-dependent over the $(r, σ_{\mathrm{init}})$ grid, supporting LoMETab as a controllable family of implicit ensembles rather than a fixed rank-1 construction.

</details>


### [93] [Turning Stale Gradients into Stable Gradients: Coherent Coordinate Descent with Implicit Landscape Smoothing for Lightweight Zeroth-Order Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14373)
*Chen Liang,Xiatao Sun,Qian Wang,Daniel Rakita*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CoCD通过将历史梯度转化为计算资产，提出了一种确定性且样本高效的零阶优化算法，在保持O(1)查询复杂度的同时，通过隐式平滑效应显著提升了收敛性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的零阶优化方法面临严重权衡：要么样本效率低（如标准有限差分法），要么因随机估计导致高方差（如随机子空间法）。因此需要一种既样本高效又具备预算意识的确定性优化策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为“相干坐标下降”（Coherent Coordinate Descent, CoCD）的零阶优化算法。该方法将零阶优化形式化为带“热启动”的块循环坐标下降（BCCD），利用历史（陈旧）梯度作为计算资产，实现每步O(1)的查询复杂度，并利用较大的有限差分步长产生隐式平滑效果以提高收敛稳定性。

Result: 在MLP、CNN和ResNet（高达27万参数）上的实验表明，CoCD在样本效率、收敛损失及准确率上显著优于BCCD，并展现出比随机零阶方法更好的稳定性。理论分析还指出较大的步长可降低有效平滑常数，从而提升收敛稳定性。

Conclusion: 确定性的结构化更新方法（如CoCD）在轻量级零阶优化场景中优于随机化方法。研究揭示了利用历史梯度信息和适当调整有限差分步长，可以有效解决零阶优化中的效率与稳定性权衡问题。

Abstract: Zeroth-Order (ZO) optimization is pivotal for scenarios where backpropagation is unavailable, such as memory-constrained on-device learning and black-box optimization. However, existing methods face a stark trade-off: they are either sample-inefficient (e.g., standard finite differences) or suffer from high variance due to randomized estimation (e.g., random subspace methods). In this work, we propose Coherent Coordinate Descent (CoCD), a deterministic, sample-efficient, and budget-aware ZO optimizer. Theoretically, we formalize the notion of gradient coherence and demonstrate that CoCD is equivalent to Block Cyclic Coordinate Descent (BCCD) with ``warm starts,'' effectively converting historical (stale) gradients from a liability into a computational asset. This mechanism enables $O(1)$ query complexity per step while maintaining global descent directions. Furthermore, we derive error bounds revealing a counter-intuitive insight: larger finite-difference step sizes can induce an implicit smoothing effect on the optimization landscape by reducing the effective smoothness constant, thereby improving convergence stability. Experiments on MLP, CNN, and ResNet architectures (up to 270k parameters) demonstrate that CoCD significantly outperforms BCCD in terms of sample efficiency and convergence loss/accuracy, and exhibits superior stability over randomized ZO methods. Our results suggest that deterministic, structure-aware updates offer a superior alternative to randomization for lightweight ZO optimization.

</details>

Method: 1. 提出“最优模式检测树”（OPDT），利用混合整数规划（MIP）技术在二分类数据中寻找单个全局最优规则；2. 引入“分支结构约束”（BSC）框架，允许用户将领域知识和业务合规性要求显式地编码进优化模型中；3. 目标函数旨在平衡规则覆盖率与误报率（假阳性率）。

Result: 实验表明，OPDT 模型在处理中等规模数据集时，能够在合理的运行时间内发现具有最优性保证的模式，有效地识别出数据中隐藏的底层规律，同时满足预设的合规性约束。

Conclusion: OPDT 是一种结合了混合整数规划的强可解释性规则发现模型，它证明了在可控的计算时间内，通过严格的数学优化手段发现全局最优模式的可行性，并为领域专家提供了将先验知识集成到模型中的有效途径。

Abstract: Pattern discovery in data plays a crucial role across diverse domains, including healthcare, risk assessment, and machinery maintenance. In contrast to black-box deep learning models, symbolic rule discovery emerges as a key data mining task, generating human-interpretable rules that offer both transparency and intuitive explainability. This paper introduces the Optimal Pattern Detection Tree (OPDT), a rule-based machine learning model based on novel mixed-integer programming to discover a single optimal pattern in data through binary classification. To incorporate prior knowledge and compliance requirements, we further introduce the Branching Structure Constraints (BSC) framework, which enables decision makers to encode domain knowledge and constraints directly into the model. This optimization-based approach discovers a hidden underlying pattern in datasets, when it exists, by identifying an optimal rule that maximizes coverage while minimizing the false positive rate due to misclassification. Our computational experiments show that OPDT discovers a pattern with optimality guarantees on moderately sized datasets within reasonable runtime.

### [95] [Data-Augmented Game Starts for Accelerating Self-Play Exploration in Imperfect Information Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14379)
*JB Lanier,Nathan Monette,Pierre Baldi,Roy Fox*

TL;DR: 该研究提出DAGS算法，通过从离线人类数据中采样起始状态来加速大规模非完美信息博弈的强化学习探索，并针对可能引入的偏差提出了修正方案，显著提升了策略求解的效率和质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模非完美信息博弈（如《星际争霸》、《Dota》等）中，由于奖励稀疏和长程时间跨度带来的探索困难，寻找近似纳什均衡在计算上极具挑战性。现有方法往往难以高效覆盖具有战略意义的子博弈，因此研究者希望利用人类专家的离线数据来引导探索，加速在线训练。

Method: 提出了一种称为“数据增强博弈起始（DAGS）”的策略，其核心思想是从高质量的离线人类示范数据中采样中间状态作为强化学习训练的起点。为解决由此产生的博弈论偏差问题，研究引入了多任务观察标志（multi-task observation flags）进行修正。此外，研究构建了一套新的基准环境，通过在现有OpenSpiel博弈中增加长程探索难度和状态空间，来评估算法性能。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过离线数据进行多智能体起始状态采样（DAGS）能有效提升大规模非完美信息博弈中的在线探索效率，同时通过多任务观察标志解决了由此带来的偏差问题。本研究提出的方法在计算资源受限的情况下，显著降低了策略的开发性（exploitability），并提供了新的基准测试环境，为解决大规模博弈中的探索难题提供了重要思路。

Abstract: Finding approximate equilibria for large-scale imperfect-information competitive games such as StarCraft, Dota, and CounterStrike remains computationally infeasible due to sparse rewards and challenging exploration over long horizons. In this paper, we propose a multi-agent starting-state sampling strategy designed to substantially accelerate online exploration in regularized policy-gradient game methods for two-player zero-sum (2p0s) games. Motivated by an assumption that offline demonstrations from skilled humans can provide good coverage of high-level strategies relevant to equilibrium play, we propose the initialization of reinforcement learning data collection at intermediate states sampled from offline data to facilitate exploration of strategically relevant subgames. Referring to this method as Data-Augmented Game Starts (DAGS), we perform experiments using synthetic datasets and analytically tractable, long-horizon control variants of two-player Kuhn Poker, Goofspiel, and a counterexample game designed to penalize biased beliefs over hidden information. Under fixed computational budgets, DAGS enables regularized policy gradient methods to achieve lower exploitability in games with significantly more challenging exploration. We show that augmenting starting state distributions when solving imperfect information games can lead to biased equilibria, and we provide a straightforward mitigation to this in the form of multi-task observation flags. Finally, we release a new set of benchmark environments that drastically increase exploration challenges and state counts in existing OpenSpiel games while keeping exploitability measurements analytically tractable.

We introduce NodeSynth, an evidence-grounded methodology that generates socially relevant synthetic queries by leveraging a fine-tuned taxonomy generator (TaG) anchored in real-world evidence. Evaluated against four mainstream LLMs (e.g., Claude 4.5 Haiku), NodeSynth elicited failure rates up to five times higher than human-authored benchmarks. In this work, we propose GeoViSTA (Geospatial Vision-Tabular Transformer), a vision-tabular architecture that learns unified geospatial embeddings from co-registered gridded imagery and tabular data. GeoViSTA utilizes bilateral cross-attention to exchange spatial and semantic information across modalities, guided by a geography-aware attention mechanism that aligns continuous image patches with irregular census-tract tokens. We train GeoViSTA with a self-supervised joint masked-autoencoding objective, forcing it to recover missing image patches and tabular rows using local spatial context and cross-modal cues. Empirically, GeoViSTA's unified embeddings improve linear probing performance on high-impact downstream tasks, outperforming baselines in predicting disease-specific mortality and fire hazard frequency across held-out regions. ### [99] [Collaborative Yet Personalized Policy Training: Single-Timescale Federated Actor-Critic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14423)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种联邦演员-评论家框架，通过让智能体共享公共线性子空间同时保持个性化策略，解决了异构环境下的协同训练难题，并从理论上证明了其具有线性加速的收敛特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种结合公共线性子空间表示与本地个性化策略组件的联邦演员-评论家框架，通过单时间尺度更新与马尔可夫采样进行协同训练；引入了联合线性近似框架、针对投影子空间更新和QR分解的扰动分析，以及处理马尔可夫噪声的条件混合论证。

Abstract: Despite the popularity of the actor-critic method and the practical needs of collaborative policy training, existing works typically either overlook environmental heterogeneity or give up personalization altogether by training a single shared policy across all agents. We consider a federated actor-critic framework in which agents share a common linear subspace representation while maintaining personalized local policy components, and agents iteratively estimate the common subspace, local critic heads, and local policies (i.e., actors). Under canonical single-timescale updates with Markovian sampling, we establish finite-time convergence via a novel joint linear approximation framework. Specifically, we show that the critic error converges to zero at the rate of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/((1-γ)^4\sqrt{TK}))$, and the policy gradient norm converges to zero at the rate of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/((1-γ)^6\sqrt{TK}))$, where $T$ is the number of rounds, $K$ is the number of agents, and $γ\in (0,1)$ is the discount factor. These results demonstrate linear speedup with respect to the number of agents $K$, despite heterogeneous Markovian trajectories under distinct transition kernels and coupled learning dynamics. To address these challenges, we develop a new perturbation analysis for the projected subspace updates and QR decomposition steps, together with conditional mixing arguments for heterogeneous Markovian noise. Furthermore, to handle the additional complications induced by policy updates and temporal dependence, we establish fine-grained characterizations of the discrepancies between function evaluations under Markovian sampling and under temporally frozen policies. Experiments instantiate the framework within PPO on federated \texttt{Hopper-v5} action-map heterogeneity, showing gains over Single PPO and FedAvg PPO and downstream transfer from the learned shared trunk.

### [100] [FrontierSmith: Synthesizing Open-Ended Coding Problems at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14445)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出自动化系统FrontierSmith，从现有的竞赛级封闭式编程题出发，通过改变目标、限制输出和泛化输入等手段迭代演化出开放式问题；引入“想法分歧度量”（idea divergence metric）筛选出能激发多样化解决方案的问题，并自动生成测试用例和验证器。

Result: 在FrontierCS和ALE-bench两个基准测试中，使用该合成数据训练的模型性能显著提升（Qwen3.5-9B和27B在相应指标上均获得大幅增长），且模型在解决问题时表现出类似人类的复杂思考过程（增加回合数和Token消耗）。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用自动化系统将封闭式编程任务演化为高质量开放式任务是可行的，这为提升大语言模型在处理复杂、开放性编程任务上的表现提供了一种高效的数据合成路径。

Abstract: Many real-world coding challenges are open-ended and admit no known optimal solution. Yet, recent progress in LLM coding has focused on well-defined tasks such as feature implementation, bug fixing, and competitive programming. Open-ended coding remains a weak spot for LLMs, largely because open-ended training problems are scarce and expensive to construct. Our goal is to synthesize open-ended coding problems at scale to train stronger LLM coders. We introduce FrontierSmith, an automated system for iteratively evolving open-ended problems from existing closed-ended coding tasks. Starting from competitive programming problems, FrontierSmith generates candidate open-ended variants by changing the problems'goals, restricting outputs, and generalizing inputs. It then uses a quantitative idea divergence metric to select problems that elicit genuinely diverse approaches from different solvers. Agents then generate test cases and verifiers for the surviving candidates. On two open-ended coding benchmarks, training on our synthesized data yields substantial gains over the base models: Qwen3.5-9B improves by +8.82 score on FrontierCS and +306.36 (Elo-rating-based performance) on ALE-bench; Qwen3.5-27B improves by +12.12 and +309.12, respectively. The synthesized problems also make agents take more turns and use more tokens, similar to human-curated ones, suggesting that closed-ended seeds can be a practical starting point for long-horizon coding data.

</details>


### [101] [When Answers Stray from Questions: Hallucination Detection via Question-Answer Orthogonal Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14449)
*Siyang Yao,Erhu Feng,Yubin Xia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了QAOD框架，通过将答案表示与问题正交化并结合Fisher特征选择，在实现高效单遍推理的同时，显著提升了大型语言模型幻觉检测的域内准确率与跨域泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型语言模型（LLM）幻觉检测方法在准确性、推理效率和跨分布稳健性之间难以取得平衡。黑盒一致性检查成本高昂，而单遍白盒探针往往因过度依赖特定领域的上下文，导致在分布外（OOD）场景下性能大幅下降。因此，亟需一种既高效又具备强泛化能力的幻觉检测方法。

Method: 提出了一种单遍（single-pass）框架“问答正交分解”（QAOD）。该方法通过将答案表示投影到问题向量的正交空间，消除问题带来的领域条件偏差；同时结合多样性惩罚的Fisher评分进行层选择，并通过Fisher重要性筛选判别性神经元。此外，设计了两种互补策略：结合问题上下文的联合探测器用于提升域内判别力，仅使用正交分量的探测器用于提升跨域（OOD）迁移表现。

Result: QAOD的联合探测器在所有评估数据集上达到了最佳的域内AUROC表现。在跨域迁移任务中，其正交分量探测器表现突出，在BioASQ数据集上较最优白盒基线提升了高达21%的性能，且计算成本不足生成成本的25%。

Conclusion: QAOD框架通过正交分解和特征选择机制，有效地平衡了大型语言模型幻觉检测中的准确性、效率与跨域稳健性。该方法证明了从答案表示中剥离问题相关信息，能够提取出更具普适性的事实信号，为解决黑盒方法成本高昂和白盒方法泛化能力弱的问题提供了有力方案。

Abstract: Hallucination detection in large language models (LLMs) requires balancing accu racy, efficiency, and robustness to distribution shift. Black-box consistency methods are effective but demand repeated inference; single-pass white-box probes are effi cient yet treat answer representations in isolation, often degrading sharply under domain shift. We propose QAOD (Question-Answer Orthogonal Decomposition), a single-pass framework that projects away the question-aligned direction from the answer representation to obtain a question-orthogonal component that suppresses domain-conditioned variation. To identify informative signals, QAOD further selects layers via diversity-penalized Fisher scoring and discriminative neurons via Fisher importance. To address both in-domain detection and cross-domain generalization, we design two complementary probing strategies: pairing the or thogonal component with question context yields a joint probe that maximizes in-domain discriminability, while using the orthogonal component alone preserves domain-agnostic factuality signals for robust transfer. QAOD's joint probe achieves the best in-domain AUROC across all evaluated model-dataset pairs, while the orthogonal-only probe delivers the strongest OOD transfer, surpassing the best white-box baseline by up to 21% on BioASQ at under 25% of generation cost.

### [102] [LiSA: Lifelong Safety Adaptation via Conservative Policy Induction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14454)
*Minbeom Kim,Lesly Miculicich,Bhavana Dalvi Mishra,Mihir Parmar,Phillip Wallis,Bharath Chandrasekhar,Kyomin Jung,Tomas Pfister,Long T. Le*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 AI 智能体在复杂部署场景下护栏失效的问题，本文提出了 LiSA 框架，通过结构化记忆和策略抽象，利用稀疏、带噪的用户反馈实现持续性的安全规则优化，有效提升了智能体的安全性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 AI 智能体介入处理私有数据、调用工具并执行多步工作流，传统的护栏机制面临重大挑战。由于安全边界往往取决于动态的上下文、组织策略及用户期望，难以在部署前穷尽规定；同时，部署反馈通常稀疏且存在噪声，频繁的微调在工程上不可行，因此迫切需要一种能够自动适应复杂运行环境并具备泛化能力的护栏更新机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为“终身安全适应”（Lifelong Safety Adaptation, LiSA）的保守策略归纳框架。该框架包含三个核心组件：1. 将偶发故障转化为可复用的策略抽象，实现从个体案例到通用规则的泛化；2. 引入冲突感知局部规则，防止在混合标注环境下的过度泛化；3. 通过后验下界实现证据感知的置信门控，确保记忆重用随着证据积累而科学扩展，而非仅仅依赖经验准确率。

Result: 在 PrivacyLens+、ConFaide+ 和 AgentHarm 等数据集的实验表明，LiSA 在稀疏反馈条件下显著优于现有的记忆基线模型；在即使高达 20% 标签错误率的噪声环境下仍保持稳健；并且在性能表现上超越了仅依靠大模型缩放（backbone model scaling）的方案，同时兼顾了低延迟需求。

Conclusion: LiSA 提供了一种在现实应用中保护 AI 智能体的有效方案，通过结构化记忆机制实现了对安全策略的持续自适应，使其能够应对不可预测的边缘风险，并有效弥补了预部署护栏在复杂多变环境下的适应性缺口。

Abstract: As AI agents move from chat interfaces to systems that read private data, call tools, and execute multi-step workflows, guardrails become a last line of defense against concrete deployment harms. In these settings, guardrail failures are no longer merely answer-quality errors: they can leak secrets, authorize unsafe actions, or block legitimate work. The hardest failures are often contextual: whether an action is acceptable depends on local privacy norms, organizational policies, and user expectations that resist pre-deployment specification. This creates a practical gap: guardrails must adapt to their own operating environments, yet deployment feedback is typically limited to sparse, noisy user-reported failures, and repeated fine-tuning is often impractical. To address this gap, we propose LiSA (Lifelong Safety Adaptation), a conservative policy induction framework that improves a fixed base guardrail through structured memory. LiSA converts occasional failures into reusable policy abstractions so that sparse reports can generalize beyond individual cases, adds conflict-aware local rules to prevent overgeneralization in mixed-label contexts, and applies evidence-aware confidence gating via a posterior lower bound, so that memory reuse scales with accumulated evidence rather than empirical accuracy alone. Across PrivacyLens+, ConFaide+, and AgentHarm, LiSA consistently outperforms strong memory-based baselines under sparse feedback, remains robust under noisy user feedback even at 20% label-flip rates, and pushes the latency--performance frontier beyond backbone model scaling. Ultimately, LiSA offers a practical path to secure AI agents against the unpredictable long tail of real-world edge risks.

Abstract: We propose a new method of learning from positive and unlabeled (PU) examples in highly imbalanced datasets. Often, training data comprises positive and unlabeled instances, the latter typically being dominated by negative, but including also several positive instances. While PU learning is well-studied, few methods address imbalanced settings or hard-to-detect positive examples that resemble negative ones. Our approach uses a focused empirical risk estimator, incorporating both positive and unlabeled examples to train binary classifiers. Empirical evaluations demonstrate state-of-the-art performance on imbalanced datasets under two labeling mechanisms - selecting positives completely at random (SCAR) and selecting at random (SAR). <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Lang2MLIP框架，将MLIP开发过程形式化为序列决策问题；利用大语言模型（LLM）作为核心智能体，根据当前的数据集、模型状态、评估结果及执行日志，动态选择优化动作，从而实现无需预定义工作流的闭环自适应开发。

Result: 在包含多种组件与界面的固体电解质界面（SEI）系统的测试中，Lang2MLIP框架表现出了良好的性能，验证了其在MLIP开发流程自动化及降低非专家使用门槛方面的可行性与潜力。

Existing automated pipelines typically assume a fixed sequence of stages or depend on domain experts, which limits their adaptability to heterogeneous materials systems where the optimal curriculum is not known in advance. To lower the barrier to developing MLIPs for non-experts, we propose Lang2MLIP, a multi-agent framework that takes natural-language input and formulates end-to-end MLIP development as a sequential decision-making problem solved by large language models (LLMs). At each step, a decision-making agent observes the current dataset, model, evaluation results, and execution log, and then automatically selects an appropriate action to improve the model. This removes the need for a predefined pipeline and enables the agent to self-correct by revisiting earlier subsystems when new failures arise. These results suggest that LLM-based multi-agent systems are a promising direction for automating MLIP development and making it more accessible to non-experts.

### [105] [Resolving Action Bottleneck: Agentic Reinforcement Learning Informed by Token-Level Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14558)
*Langzhou He,Junyou Zhu,Yue Zhou,Zhengyao Gu,Junhua Liu,Wei-Chieh Huang,Henry Peng Zou,David Wipf,Philip S. Yu,Qitian Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现智能体学习中存在“动作瓶颈”，即推理标记占用了过多的梯度信用。作者提出了 ActFocus 方法，通过重新加权标记并聚焦于关键动作，显著提升了智能体的训练效率和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的策略梯度算法（如 PPO、GRPO）在智能体强化学习中对所有标记执行统一的信用分配，导致训练信号被错误地分配在大量的推理标记上，而忽略了核心的动作标记，进而限制了模型在复杂任务中的表现。

Method: 1. 基于能量模型视角，分析了标记级别的训练信号分配问题。
2. 提出 ActFocus 方法：通过降低推理标记的梯度权重，并结合基于能量的重分配机制，根据不确定性进一步增加动作标记的权重。

Result: 在四个基准环境中，ActFocus 在不同模型规模下均一致优于 PPO 和 GRPO，性能提升最高分别达到 65.2 和 63.7 个百分点，且未增加额外的运行时或内存开销。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了智能体强化学习中存在的“动作瓶颈”现象，即现有的策略梯度方法对推理标记和动作标记同等对待，导致训练信号分配不当。通过简单的标记加权策略 ActFocus，可以在不增加计算开销的前提下显著提升模型性能，为智能体模型的优化提供了一种高效的新范式。

Abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning trains large language models using multi-turn trajectories that interleave long reasoning traces with short environment-facing actions. Common policy-gradient methods, such as PPO and GRPO, treat each token in a trajectory equally, leading to uniform credit assignment. In this paper, we critically demonstrate that such uniform credit assignment largely misallocates token-level training signals. From an energy-based modeling perspective, we show that token-level training signals, quantified by their correlations with reward variance of different rollouts sampled from a given prompt, concentrate sharply on action tokens rather than reasoning tokens, even though action tokens account for only a small fraction of the trajectory. We refer to this phenomenon as the Action Bottleneck. Motivated by this observation, we propose an embarrassingly simple token reweighting approach, ActFocus, that downweights gradients on reasoning tokens, along with an additional energy-based redistribution mechanism that further increases the weights on action tokens with higher uncertainty. Across four environments and different model sizes, ActFocus consistently outperforms PPO and GRPO, yielding final-step gains of up to 65.2 and 63.7 percentage points, respectively, without any additional runtime or memory cost.

</details>

### [107] [RxEval: A Prescription-Level Benchmark for Evaluating LLM Medication Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14543)
*Shuhao Chen,Weisen Jiang,Changmiao Wang,Xiaoqing Wu,Xuanren Shi,Yu Zhang,James T. Kwok*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 RxEval，这是一个针对住院用药推荐的处方级评测基准。通过更细致的患者时序数据和推理干扰项，发现当前大语言模型在准确开具用药、剂量和途径方面仍存在显著的推理障碍和信息处理缺失。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 RxEval 处方级医疗基准。该基准将处方任务建模为多选题，通过详尽的患者档案和按时间排序的临床轨迹来模拟真实处方环境。同时，利用推理链扰动技术构建了患者特定的干扰项，旨在精准评估模型在选择具体药物、剂量和给药途径方面的准确性。

Conclusion: RxEval 揭示了现有大语言模型在临床处方任务中仍面临显著挑战，模型往往难以充分利用患者信息并进行逻辑推理。该基准为未来开发更具临床应用价值的医疗辅助 AI 模型提供了重要的评估手段。

Abstract: Inpatient medication recommendation requires clinicians to repeatedly select specific medications, doses, and routes as a patient's condition evolves. Existing benchmarks formulate this task as admission-level prediction over coarse drug codes with multi-hot diagnostic and procedure code inputs, failing to capture the per-timepoint, information-rich nature of real prescribing. We propose RxEval, a prescription-level benchmark that evaluates LLM prescribing capability by multiple-choice questions: each question presents a detailed patient profile and time-ordered clinical trajectory, requiring selection of specific medication-dose-route triples from real prescriptions and patient-specific distractors generated via reasoning-chain perturbation. RxEval comprises 1,547 questions spanning 584 patients, 18 diagnostic categories, and 969 unique medications. Evaluation of 16 LLMs shows that RxEval is both challenging and discriminative: F1 ranges from 45.18 to 77.10 across models, and the best Exact Match is only 46.10%. Error analysis reveals that even frontier models may overlook stated patient information and fail to derive clinical conclusions.

### [108] [Multi-Dimensional Model Integrity and Responsibility Assessment Index and Scoring Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14550)
*Phuc Truong Loc Nguyen,Thanh Hung Do,Truong Thanh Hung Nguyen,Hung Cao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了MIRAI评估框架，旨在综合衡量表格模型在可解释性、公平性、稳健性、隐私和可持续性方面的表现，揭示了高性能模型并不等同于负责任模型，并为受监管环境下的模型筛选提供了统一标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医疗、金融等高风险表格数据领域，仅关注预测性能是不够的。现有的评估方法通常将可解释性、公平性、稳健性、隐私和可持续性等关键维度孤立评估，缺乏一个统一的框架来权衡这些维度，导致难以在这些关键指标之间做出全面的选择。

Method: 提出了“模型完整性与责任评估指数”（MIRAI）。该框架整合了可解释性、公平性、稳健性、隐私保护和可持续性五个维度，通过标准化和方向对齐的指标处理，将多维评估汇总为单一得分，从而在受控环境下实现跨模型架构的直接对比。

Result: 实验表明，预测性能与模型的整体完整性和责任性之间不存在必然的线性正相关。在多个案例中，简单的模型在五个维度之间实现了比复杂的深度表格架构更优的平衡。

Conclusion: 在受到严格监管的领域（如医疗、金融），盲目追求高预测性能是不够的。MIRAI框架揭示了复杂模型在整体模型完整性与责任性上并不总是优于简单模型，为负责任的模型选择提供了一个实用且全面的评估依据。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence in high-stakes tabular domains cannot be evaluated by predictive performance alone, yet current practice still assesses explainability, fairness, robustness, privacy, and sustainability mostly in isolation. We propose the Model Integrity and Responsibility Assessment Index (MIRAI), a unified evaluation framework that measures tabular models across these five dimensions under a controlled comparison setting and aggregates them into a single score. MIRAI combines established metrics through normalized and direction-aligned dimension scores, which enables direct comparison across models with different architectural and computational profiles. Experiments on healthcare, financial, and socioeconomic datasets show that higher predictive performance does not necessarily imply better overall integrity and responsibility. In several cases, simpler models achieve a stronger cross-dimensional balance than more complex deep tabular architectures. MIRAI provides a compact and practical basis for responsible model selection in regulated settings.

</details>


### [109] [SeesawNet: Towards Non-stationary Time Series Forecasting with Balanced Modeling of Common and Specific Dependencies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14551)
*Hao Li,Lu Zhang,Liu Chong,Yankai Chen,Pengyang Wang,Yingjie Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SeesawNet 通过引入自适应注意力机制，在非平稳时间序列预测中动态融合了“全局公共依赖”与“局部特定依赖”，有效解决了归一化带来的信息丢失问题，并实现了更高的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实例归一化（IN）虽能减少分布偏移，但也抹杀了对建模时间序列异质性至关重要的实例特定结构信息。现有的改进方法未能有效解决如何在保持全局共性与捕捉实例特定性之间找到动态平衡的矛盾。

Method: 提出了 SeesawNet 架构，核心是自适应平稳-非平稳注意力机制（ASNA）。ASNA 通过从归一化序列提取公共依赖，从原始序列提取特定依赖，并根据实例的非平稳性程度动态融合两者。在此基础上，模型交替执行时间维度和通道维度的关系建模。

Result: 在多个真实世界的时间序列预测基准测试中，SeesawNet 的预测性能均显著优于现有的前沿（SOTA）方法。

Conclusion: SeesawNet 通过动态平衡公共依赖与实例特定依赖，成功克服了传统实例归一化（IN）在处理非平稳时间序列时导致的过度平滑问题，为时间序列预测提供了一种更具鲁棒性和适应性的新框架。

Abstract: Instance normalization (IN) is widely used in non-stationary multivariate time series forecasting to reduce distribution shifts and highlight common patterns across samples. However, IN can over-smooth instance-specific structural information that is essential for modeling temporal and cross-channel heterogeneity. While prior methods further suppress distribution discrepancies or attempt to recover temporal specific dependencies, they often ignore a central tension: how to adaptively model common and instance-specific dependency based on each instance's non-stationary structures. To address this dilemma, we propose SeesawNet, a unified architecture that dynamically balances common and instance-specific dependency modeling in both temporal and channel dimensions. At its core is Adaptive Stationary-Nonstationary Attention (ASNA), which captures common dependencies from normalized sequences and specific dependencies from raw sequences, and adaptively fuses them according to instance-level non-stationarity. Built upon ASNA, SeesawNet alternates dedicated temporal and channel relationship modeling to jointly capture long-range and cross-variable dependencies. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world benchmarks demonstrate that SeesawNet consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods.

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has achieved great success in developing Large Language Models (LLMs) with chain-of-thought rollouts for many tasks such as math and coding. Nevertheless, RLVR struggles with sample efficiency on difficult problems where correct rollouts are hard to generate. We find that three components are vital for the success: supervised signal, on-policy signal, and decaying weights on the few-shot SFT dataset to prevent overfitting from multiple-epoch training. Casting the problem into the pure-exploration bandits framework, we adapt provably efficient algorithms from multi-objective bandits and further introduce a novel design for best feasible arm identification in structured bandits, with theoretical guarantees on the identification error in the linear case. ### [112] [Woodelf++: A Fast and Unified Partial Dependence Plot Algorithm for Decision Tree Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14578)
*Ron Wettenstein,Alexander Nadel,Udi Boker*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Woodelf++ 是一种针对决策树集成模型的高效可解释性框架，它通过创新的伪布尔函数计算方法，实现了 PDP、Joint-PDP 和任意阶 PDIV 的极速计算，相比现有方案性能提升可达数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 PDP（偏依赖图）、Joint-PDP 和 PDIV（偏依赖交互值）计算方法在处理大规模数据集或高阶交互时计算开销巨大。为了解决这些计算瓶颈，研究者旨在开发一种统一且极其高效的算法，以在决策树集成模型中实现对任意特征子集交互的高效解释。

Method: Woodelf++ 基于之前的高效 SHAP 计算算法 Woodelf，通过在伪布尔函数上推导适当的指标，将 PDP、Joint-PDP 和任意阶 PDIV 的计算统一到一个框架下。此外，它利用决策树的分割阈值引入了“全 PDP”（Full PDP）计算方法，支持纯 Python 实现并具备 GPU 加速能力。

Result: Woodelf++ 在处理 40 万行数据集时表现出色：PDP 和 Joint-PDP 的计算速度比现有先进方法快 6 倍，比 scikit-learn 快 5 个数量级；在任意阶 PDIV 计算上，Woodelf++ 仅需 5 分钟即可完成，而现有方法预计需要 100 万年以上，实现了数量级上的性能突破。

Conclusion: Woodelf++ 是一个高效、统一的决策树集成模型可解释性工具框架。它通过在伪布尔函数上推导指标，不仅显著提升了 PDP、Joint-PDP 和任意阶 PDIV 的计算效率，还提出了“全 PDP”（Full PDP）概念，为模型行为分析提供了更精准的手段。该方法在实际应用中展现了跨越数量级的性能提升，为大规模数据集上的复杂解释任务提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Partial Dependence Plots (PDPs) visualize how changes in a single feature affect the average model prediction. They are widely used in practice to interpret decision tree ensembles and other machine learning models. Joint-PDPs extend this idea to pairs of features, revealing their combined effect. Partial Dependence Interaction Values (PDIVs) measure feature interactions. The Any-Order-PDIVs task computes these interactions for every feature subset across all rows of the dataset.
  We introduce Woodelf++, a unified and efficient approach for computing all these useful explainability tools on decision tree ensembles, building on Woodelf, an algorithm for efficient SHAP computation. By deriving suitable metrics over pseudo-Boolean functions, Woodelf++ can compute PDPs (exact and approximate), Joint-PDPs, and Any-Order-PDIVs in a unified framework. Our method delivers substantial complexity improvements over the state of the art, including an exponential gain for Any-Order-PDIVs. Additionally, we introduce and efficiently compute Full PDPs, which leverage the model's split thresholds to faithfully capture its behavior across all possible feature values.
  Woodelf++ is implemented in pure Python and supports GPU acceleration. On a dataset with 400,000 rows, Woodelf++ computes PDP and Joint-PDP up to 6x faster than the state of the art and up to five orders of magnitude faster than scikit-learn. For Any-Order-PDIVs, the gap is even larger: Woodelf++ computes all interaction values in 5 minutes, while the state of the art is estimated to require over 1,000,000 years.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对14,664个案例进行实证研究，涵盖了多种主流的可塑性干预措施和后门攻击场景；通过病理分析（Pathological analysis）探究了干预措施影响后门威胁的具体机理（如梯度放大、激活路径中断及表征空间压缩）。

Result: 研究发现除SAM（锐度感知最小化）外，大多数可塑性干预措施能减轻后门威胁；SAM的加剧作用源于后门梯度的放大，而其他措施的缓解作用则源于激活路径的破坏和表征空间的压缩。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了可塑性干预措施与DRL后门攻击之间的复杂相互作用，建立了SCC框架以指导稳健的后门注入，并提出利用损失函数地形的锐度（sharpness）作为检测DRL后门攻击的关键指标。

Abstract: Extensive research has highlighted the severe threats posed by backdoor attacks to deep reinforcement learning (DRL). However, prior studies primarily focus on vanilla scenarios, while plasticity interventions have emerged as indispensable built-in components of modern DRL agents. Despite their effectiveness in mitigating plasticity loss, the impact of these interventions on DRL backdoor vulnerabilities remains underexplored, and this lack of systematic investigation poses risks in practical DRL deployments. To bridge this gap, we empirically study 14,664 cases integrating representative interventions and attack scenarios. We find that only one intervention (i.e., SAM) exacerbates backdoor threats, while other interventions mitigate them. Pathological analysis identifies that the exacerbation is attributed to backdoor gradient amplification, while the mitigation stems from activation pathway disruption and representation space compression. From these findings, we derive two novel insights: (1) a conceptual framework SCC for robust backdoor injection that deconstructs the mechanistic interplay between interventions and backdoors in DRL, and (2) abnormal loss landscape sharpness as a key indicator for DRL backdoor detection.

Abstract: Adaptations of features commonly applied in the field of visual computing, co-occurrence matrix (COM) and run-length matrix (RLM), are proposed for the similarity computation of strings in general (words, phrases, codes and texts). Other statistical measures that are commonly employed in the field such as longest common subsequence, maximal consecutive longest common subsequence, mutual information and edit distances are evaluated and compared. ### [115] [Silent Collapse in Recursive Learning Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14588)
*Zhipeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了递归训练中传统评估指标无法发现的“沉默坍缩”现象，提出了基于表征轨迹早期预警信号的MTR框架，在不依赖原始数据的前提下，实现了模型内部退化的主动监控与预防。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归学习在大型语言模型和自主智能体中日益普及，但传统的评估指标（如损失函数、准确率）无法及时发现模型内部发生的不可逆退化，导致潜在的系统性故障。研究旨在量化这种“沉默坍缩”并提供早期预警与预防机制。

Method: 1. 识别并定义了“沉默坍缩”（Silent Collapse）现象，即模型内部概率分布、表征多样性及长尾覆盖率在传统性能指标下降前发生收缩。
2. 提炼出三个轨迹级预警指标：锚点熵收缩、表征漂移冻结以及长尾覆盖率侵蚀。
3. 提出MTR（监控-信任-调节）框架：一个元认知循环，通过监控轨迹统计数据，动态调节学习强度，以规避模型坍缩。

Result: 实验表明，在传统评估指标表现稳定甚至提升的情况下，模型内部的表征多样性和长尾覆盖能力早已开始退化。MTR框架能够比标准验证指标提前数代捕捉到坍缩征兆，并有效通过调节学习强度延长模型的有效递归周期，而无需访问原始数据。

Conclusion: 递归训练中存在的“沉默坍缩”问题是导致模型性能隐性退化的核心风险。通过MTR框架，可以在不依赖原始数据的情况下，通过监控表征轨迹的早期预警信号，主动干预并防止模型内部结构的坍缩，从而确保递归系统的长期稳定与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Recursive learning -- where models are trained on data generated by previous versions of themselves -- is increasingly common in large language models, autonomous agents, and self-supervised systems. However, standard performance metrics (loss, perplexity, accuracy) often fail to detect internal degradation before it becomes irreversible. Here we identify a phenomenon we call silent collapse: under broad recursive conditions, model internal distributions -- predictive entropy, representational diversity, and tail coverage -- progressively contract even as conventional metrics appear stable or improving.
  We discover that silent collapse is not abrupt. Its onset is reliably preceded by three trajectory-level precursors: (1) contraction of anchor entropy, (2) freezing of representation drift, and (3) erosion of tail coverage. These signals manifest multiple generations before any degradation in standard validation metrics, enabling early warning.
  Based on these precursors, we propose the MTR (Monitor--Trust--Regulator) framework, a lightweight metacognitive loop that monitors trajectory statistics, estimates a slow-timescale trust variable, and adaptively modulates the effective learning intensity. MTR provides early warning and actively prevents silent collapse without requiring access to pristine real data -- a critical advantage when original data is unavailable, contaminated, or private.

### [116] [Forgetting That Sticks: Quantization-Permanent Unlearning via Circuit Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15138)
*Saisab Sadhu,Pratinav Seth,Vinay Kumar Sankarapu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了机器遗忘在量化模型下的失效困境，并提出了一种基于机械归因与零空间投影的新方法 MANSU，成功解决了遗忘在量化后失效或破坏模型性能的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘评估忽略了量化（PTQ）的影响，研究发现 4-bit 量化会导致遗忘失效或导致模型性能崩溃。作者将此归因于“稀疏性-持久性权衡”，即过小的梯度更新无法跨越量化边界，导致遗忘失效。

Method: 提出 MANSU (Mechanistic-Aligned Null-Space Unlearning)，通过因果回路归因定位遗忘集子图，结合回路限制的零空间投影与费舍尔信息保留约束，并引入参数量级下限以确保更新幅度足以越过量化桶边界。此外，引入电路归因散度 (CAD) 评估结构化遗忘。

Result: 实验表明，现有梯度基准在量化后会发生遗忘恢复（准确率提升约 0.05）。相比之下，MANSU 在多模型族和基准测试中，在实现有效遗忘、保持保留集性能、抗量化失效以及实现结构化擦除这四个维度上均取得了显著优势。

Conclusion: MANSU 通过将解耦的结构化擦除与针对量化鲁棒性的参数约束相结合，首次实现了在保持模型性能的同时，确保持久、结构化的机器遗忘，克服了现有梯度方法在量化环境下的失效问题。

Abstract: Standard unlearning evaluations measure behavioral suppression in full precision, immediately after training, despite every deployed language model being quantized first. Recent work has shown that 4-bit post-training quantization can reverse machine unlearning; we show this is not a tuning artefact but a systematic dual failure: gradient-based methods that achieve meaningful forgetting lose it under compression, while methods that survive quantization barely change the model. Both failures trace to the same root cause: across all baselines, per-parameter updates lie 47-828x below the NF4 quantization bin width; updates diffused across billions of parameters cannot clear quantization bin boundaries, a consequence we formalize as a sparsity-permanence tradeoff. We present MANSU (Mechanistic-Aligned Null-Space Unlearning), which resolves both modes by combining causal circuit attribution to isolate the minimal forget-set subgraph, circuit-restricted null-space projection with a diagonal-Fisher retain bound, and a per-parameter magnitude floor guaranteeing quantization survival by construction. We additionally introduce Circuit Attribution Divergence (CAD), a mechanistic verification metric distinguishing structural erasure from behavioral suppression, a distinction existing metrics cannot make. Across multiple model families and hazard benchmarks, MANSU is the first method to jointly satisfy all four properties with margin on each (meaningful forgetting, retain preservation, non-positive PTQ gap, and structural erasure), while gradient-based baselines recover up to +0.05 accuracy under compression.

</details>


### [117] [Fast Rates for Inverse Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14599)
*Andreas Schlaginhaufen,Maryam Kamgarpour*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对Borel空间下的熵正则化Min-Max逆强化学习，证明了其与最大似然估计的等价性，并利用损失函数的伪自协调性，推导出参数和策略学习在模型错误指定下可达到的O(1/n)快速收敛速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的逆强化学习理论通常受限于有限状态空间或需要严格的探索假设。本文旨在解决更通用的Borel状态与动作空间下的Min-Max-IRL理论问题，填补其在结构等价性、统计收敛速度以及模型错误指定处理方面的理论空白。

Method: 本文结合了凸分析、信息几何和优化理论，具体包括：1.利用伪自协调性（pseudo-self-concordance）分析Min-Max-IRL损失函数的性质；2.在一般Borel空间下推导软最优值函数（soft-optimal value function）对奖励参数的导数；3.基于Hessian范数进行统计误差分析，证明了轨迹级KL散度和参数误差的收敛性。

Result: 1.证明了在总体水平下，Min-Max-IRL与MLE的等价性，以及在确定性动力学下的经验等价性。2.建立了参数估计和策略学习的统计收敛边界，实现了O(1/n)的快速收敛率。3.推广了奖励可识别性结果至Borel空间，并推导了软最优值函数的相关导数公式，为该类算法的稳健性提供了理论支持。

Conclusion: 本文确立了熵正则化最小-最大逆强化学习（Min-Max-IRL）在一般Borel状态空间下的理论基础。研究证明了该方法在总体水平上与最大似然估计（MLE）的等价性，并为该框架提供了强大的统计收敛保证，证明了即使在模型错误指定的情况下，学习到的策略和奖励参数也能达到O(1/n)的快速收敛速率。

Abstract: We establish novel structural and statistical results for entropy-regularized min-max inverse reinforcement learning (Min-Max-IRL) with linear reward classes in finite-horizon MDPs with Borel state and action spaces. On the structural side, we show that maximum likelihood estimation (MLE) and Min-Max-IRL are equivalent at the population level, and at the empirical level under deterministic dynamics. On the statistical side, exploiting pseudo-self-concordance of the Min-Max-IRL loss, we prove that both the trajectory-level KL divergence and the squared parameter error in the Hessian norm decay at the fast rate $\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$, where $n$ is the number of expert trajectories. Our guarantees apply under misspecification and require no exploration assumptions. We further extend reward-identifiability results to general Borel spaces and derive novel results on the derivatives of the soft-optimal value function with respect to reward parameters.

### [118] [Self-Distilled Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15155)
*Zhengxi Lu,Zhiyuan Yao,Zhuowen Han,Zi-Han Wang,Jinyang Wu,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Weiming Lu,Jun Xiao,Yueting Zhuang,Yongliang Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SDAR 是一种创新的强化学习辅助框架，通过引入门控机制对 token 级监督信号进行精细化过滤，解决了长程智能体训练中自蒸馏信号不稳定及负面偏见的问题，显著提升了 LLM 智能体在多任务下的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 智能体强化学习（如 GRPO）通常依赖轨迹级的奖励信号，在长程任务中监督过于粗糙。虽然在线自蒸馏（OPSD）能提供更密集的 token 级指导，但在多轮交互中容易受到不稳定性和技能检索偏差的影响，导致监督信号质量下降。因此，研究人员希望设计一种既能利用细粒度监督信号，又能保持强化学习稳定性的优化方法。

Method: 提出了“自蒸馏智能体强化学习”（SDAR）。该方法以强化学习（RL）为核心优化基石，将 OPSD 作为一种带门控机制（gated auxiliary objective）的辅助目标引入。通过 sigmoid 门控函数将脱离的 token 级信号映射处理，仅在教师模型正面认可的 token 上强化蒸馏，并对教师可能存在的负面拒绝信号进行平滑衰减，从而避免了传统自蒸馏方法在多轮交互中的不稳定性和偏见。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5 和 Qwen3 模型系列上的实验表明，SDAR 在 ALFWorld、WebShop 和 Search-QA 等任务上表现优异。相较于基准方法 GRPO，SDAR 在 ALFWorld 上提升了 9.4%，Search-QA 上提升了 7.0%，WebShop 上提升了 10.2%，且在不同模型规模下均表现出比传统混合 RL-OPSD 方法更强的稳定性和性能。

Conclusion: SDAR 通过将在线自蒸馏（OPSD）作为受控的辅助目标集成到强化学习中，有效解决了长程多轮交互中蒸馏信号的不稳定性和误导性问题。该方法证明了在保持强化学习作为核心优化目标的同时，引入精细的 token 级监督可以显著提升 LLM 智能体的性能，为复杂任务中的策略优化提供了更稳健的范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a central paradigm for post-training LLM agents, yet its trajectory-level reward signal provides only coarse supervision for long-horizon interaction. On-Policy Self-Distillation (OPSD) complements RL by introducing dense token-level guidance from a teacher branch augmented with privileged context. However, transferring OPSD to multi-turn agents proves problematic: compounding multi-turn instability destabilizes supervision, while skill-conditioned privileged guidance requires asymmetric treatment for negative teacher rejections may arise from imperfect skills retrieval or utilization. We introduce SDAR (Self-Distilled Agentic Reinforcement Learning), which treats OPSD as a gated auxiliary objective while keeping RL as the primary optimization backbone. SDAR maps detached token-level signals into a sigmoid gate, strengthening distillation on teacher-endorsed positive-gap tokens and softly attenuating negative teacher rejections. Across the Qwen2.5 and Qwen3 families on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Search-QA, SDAR substantially improves over GRPO (+9.4% on ALFWorld, +7.0% on Search-QA, +10.2% on WebShop-Acc), avoids the instability of naive GRPO+OPSD, and consistently outperforms hybrid RL--OPSD baselines across model scales.

### [119] [An Amortized Efficiency Threshold for Comparing Neural and Heuristic Solvers in Combinatorial Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14624)
*Sohaib Afifi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文挑战了“神经组合优化求解器能效低”的传统认知，提出了AET（摊销效率阈值）框架来量化部署规模对能效评估的影响，证明了在高规模部署下，神经求解器在能源和碳排放方面比传统启发式算法更具优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对神经组合优化求解器因训练GPU能耗高而常被批评为能效低下的现象，作者指出这一批评忽略了推理阶段的成本差异，旨在通过构建数学框架来界定神经求解器与传统CPU启发式算法在何种部署规模下更具能效优势。

Method: 作者定义了“摊销效率阈值”（AET），量化了神经求解器在达到特定部署规模时，在满足解质量约束下与启发式基准（HGS via PyVRP）实现能源或碳排放平衡的临界点。此外，研究构建了包含硬件制造隐含碳的评估模型，并在多任务车辆路径问题（MTVRP）上进行了实证测量。

Result: 在n=20规模的MTVRP环境下，神经求解器的盈亏平衡点（AET）约为1.58×10^5个部署实例，且单实例能耗比为0.41。这表明当部署量超过该阈值时，神经求解器的总能耗将低于启发式算法。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了“神经求解器因训练能耗高而低效”这一观点在特定部署规模下是不成立的。通过引入AET框架，研究明确了神经求解器在达到一定部署规模后，其总能源和碳排放优势会显现，为神经组合优化器的实际应用提供了科学的能效评估准则。

Abstract: A common critique of neural combinatorial-optimization solvers is that they are less energy-efficient than CPU metaheuristics, given the operational energy cost of training them on GPUs. This paper examines the inferential step from "training is expensive" to "neural solvers are net-inefficient", which is where the critique actually goes wrong. Training the network costs a large fixed amount of GPU energy; running the metaheuristic costs a small amount of CPU energy on every instance, repeated as long as the solver is deployed. The two are not commensurable until a deployment volume is fixed. We define the Amortized Efficiency Threshold (AET) as the deployment volume above which a neural solver breaks even with a heuristic baseline in total energy or carbon, under an explicit constraint on solution quality. We show that the cumulative-energy ratio between the two solvers tends to a constant strictly below one whenever the network wins per-instance, and that this limit does not depend on how the training cost was measured. An embodied-carbon term amortizes hardware fabrication symmetrically on both sides. We instantiate the framework on the Multi-Task VRP (MTVRP) environment at n=20 customers across 19 problem variants and five training seeds, with HGS via PyVRP as the heuristic baseline. The measured crossover sits near $1.58 \times 10^5$ deployed instances; the per-instance ratio is 0.41, reflecting the moderate size of the instances tested. The contribution is the framework, the open instrumentation, and the measurement protocol; structural convergence of the ratio at larger problem sizes is left to future empirical work.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: FutureSim 提供了一个评估 AI 智能体在开放世界中适应动态环境能力的基准，揭示了当前顶尖模型在预测未来真实世界事件方面的局限性。该基准为研究长跨度测试时适应、检索、记忆和不确定性推理提供了有效的试验场。

Abstract: AI agents are being increasingly deployed in dynamic, open-ended environments that require adapting to new information as it arrives. To efficiently measure this capability for realistic use-cases, we propose building grounded simulations that replay real-world events in the order they occurred. We build FutureSim, where agents forecast world events beyond their knowledge cutoff while interacting with a chronological replay of the world: real news articles arriving and questions resolving over the simulated period. We evaluate frontier agents in their native harness, testing their ability to predict world events over a three-month period from January to March 2026. FutureSim reveals a clear separation in their capabilities, with the best agent's accuracy being 25%, and many having worse Brier skill score than making no prediction at all. Through careful ablations, we show how FutureSim offers a realistic setting to study emerging research directions like long-horizon test-time adaptation, search, memory, and reasoning about uncertainty. Overall, we hope our benchmark design paves the way to measure AI progress on open-ended adaptation spanning long time-horizons in the real world.

### [121] [Unbiased and Second-Order-Free Training for High-Dimensional PDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14643)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种新的无偏、免二阶导数的训练框架，旨在消除欧拉-丸山（EM）离散化带来的损失函数偏差，同时避免了使用Heun等高阶方案所带来的高昂计算成本。

Abstract: Deep learning methods based on backward stochastic differential equations (BSDEs) have emerged as competitive alternatives to physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) for solving high-dimensional partial differential equations (PDEs). By leveraging probabilistic representations, BSDE approaches can avoid the curse of dimensionality and often admit second-order-free training objectives that do not require explicit Hessian evaluations. It has recently been established that the commonly used Euler-Maruyama (EM) time discretization induces an intrinsic bias in BSDE training losses. While high-order schemes such as Heun can fully eliminate this bias, such schemes re-introduce second-order spatial derivatives and incur substantial computational overhead. In this work, we provide a principled analysis of EM-induced loss bias and propose an unbiased, second-order-free training framework that preserves the computational advantages of BSDE methods. Our code is available at https://github.com/seojaemin22/Un-EM-BSDE.

### [122] [Slower Generalization, Faster Memorization: A Sweet Spot in Algorithmic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14659)
*Shin So,Kyelim Lee,Albert No*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，在结构化输出任务（如NW矩阵生成）中，增加训练数据量并不总能加速模型的泛化收敛。研究发现存在一个“数据规模最佳点”，超出此范围后，模型学习效率反而下降，这揭示了规则学习与拟合效率之间存在的独特权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 既有的关于grokking（突现泛化）的临界数据量解释认为，一旦数据量足以识别底层规则，增加数据应能加速验证集收敛。作者旨在验证这一直觉在结构化输出任务中是否成立，并探索泛化与训练收敛之间的复杂关系。

Method: 研究者选择了Needleman-Wunsch (NW) 矩阵生成任务作为受控的结构化输出基准，并与乘法运算任务进行对比。通过控制训练数据集的大小，观察小规模Transformer模型在验证集精确匹配准确率达到高水平所需的梯度更新次数，从而评估不同数据规模下的收敛行为。

Result: 在NW任务中，存在一个“最佳数据规模”点，超过该点后，虽然泛化仍然可行，但模型需要更多的梯度更新才能达到高准确率。这与乘法基准任务的表现不同，证明了训练效率并非随数据量增加而单调优化，且存在学习规则与完全拟合目标之间的非线性权衡。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在某些结构化输出任务中，泛化所需的临界数据量与优化训练收敛速度所需的数据量并不一致。这揭示了学习规则与实现完美拟合之间存在差异，并挑战了“更多数据总是能加速验证集收敛”的直觉。

Abstract: Critical-data-size accounts of grokking suggest a natural post-threshold intuition: once training data is sufficient to identify the underlying rule, additional data should accelerate validation convergence. We show that this intuition can fail in a controlled structured-output task. In Needleman--Wunsch (NW) matrix generation, small Transformers reach high validation exact-match accuracy fastest at an intermediate dataset size, not at the largest one. Past this dataset-size sweet spot, generalization remains achievable but requires more gradient updates. Conversely, in the regime where partial validation competence first appears, larger datasets can require fewer updates to reach high training accuracy, suggesting that emerging rule structure can accelerate fitting beyond example-wise memorization. A multiplication baseline does not show the same post-threshold slowdown. These results separate the critical data size for the onset of generalization from the dataset size that optimizes update-based convergence, and identify structured-output tasks where learning the rule and completing exact-fitting can diverge.

### [123] [AQKA: Active Quantum Kernel Acquisition Under a Shot Budget](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14672)
*Jian Xu,Chao Li,Delu Zeng,John Paisley,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对量子核学习中测量预算不足的问题，本文提出了AQKA算法，通过理论推导出的非均匀射击分配策略，在减少测量开销的同时，显著提升了核方法在近邻量子硬件上的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子核估计（QKE）方法在面对大规模数据时，测量射击次数（shots）的需求量巨大，成为近邻量子硬件部署的主要瓶颈。现有的预算节省方法虽然优化了测量哪些条目，但在分配射击次数时仍采用均匀分配，忽视了不同核矩阵条目对下游分类器性能的影响程度。作者旨在填补这一空白，通过理论引导的非均匀分配来提升受限资源下的学习性能。

Method: 1. 提出了AQKA（自适应量子核对齐）算法，该算法摒弃了传统的均匀射击分配策略。
2. 推导了闭式的对级（pair-level）获取理论，明确了最优射击分配比例 $s_{ij}^{\star} \propto |g_{ij}|\sqrt{K_{ij}(1-K_{ij})}$，其中 $g_{ij}$ 针对核岭回归（KRR）和支持向量机（SVM）分别给出了具体梯度表达式。
3. 建立了稀疏感知下的Cauchy--Schwarz界限，并提供了显式常数的后悔界限。
4. 在多台IBM量子处理器上进行了在线自适应分配实验验证。

Result: 1. 在资源受限的核岭回归任务中，AQKA在$N=225$到$N=1000$的规模上，表现出比均匀分配高出8至25个百分点的性能提升。
2. 在156量子比特的IBM硬件上，AQKA实现了26至32个百分点的性能增益。
3. 在IBM实际量子硬件（aachen和berlin）上的在线实验中，AQKA相比均匀策略实现了显著的准确率提升（约14-17个百分点）。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入AQKA算法，证明了在受限预算下，非均匀的测量分配策略能显著超越传统的均匀分配策略。AQKA通过闭式理论优化预算分配，为近邻量子硬件上的量子核学习提供了一种高效、可扩展且在实际硬件上得到验证的解决方案。

Abstract: Estimating an $N \times N$ quantum kernel from circuit fidelities requires $Θ(N^2 S)$ measurement shots, the dominant bottleneck for deployment on near-term hardware. Existing budget-saving methods (Nyström-QKE, ShoFaR, kernel-target alignment) sub-sample \emph{which} entries to measure but allocate shots \emph{uniformly} within their chosen subset, ignoring how much each entry drives the downstream classifier. We close this gap with two contributions. \textbf{First, a complete regime decomposition} for shot-budgeted quantum kernel learning: a principled menu of when each allocator wins. Our method, \emph{AQKA}, dominates the budget-limited regime ($B \lesssim 16 n_{\mathrm{pairs}}$) on sparse-sensitivity KRR, with the gap \emph{growing} from $+8$ to $+25$ pts over uniform as $N$ scales $225{\to}1000$ and reaching $+26$--$32$ pts on an \texttt{ibm\_pittsburgh} (156-qubit Heron) hardware kernel; Nyström-QKE wins at saturating budgets on planted-sparse via low-rank reconstruction; ShoFaR is competitive only at extreme low budgets. \textbf{Second, a closed-form pair-level acquisition theory}: $s_{ij}^{\star} \propto |g_{ij}|\sqrt{K_{ij}(1-K_{ij})}$ with explicit gradient $g_{ij}$ for KRR (Lemma~1, $|β_iα_j+β_jα_i|\sqrt{K_{ij}(1-K_{ij})}$) and SVM via the envelope theorem ($|η_i^*η_j^*|\sqrt{K_{ij}(1-K_{ij})}$); a \emph{corrected} sparsity-aware Cauchy--Schwarz rate $ρ\le 2m/N$ matching empirics (vs.\ the naive $m^2/N^2$); an explicit-constant plug-in regret bound (Theorem~2); and a tighter SVM ceiling $ρ^{\mathrm{SVM}} \le m_{\mathrm{sv}}^2/N^2$. We close with the first multi-seed live online adaptive shot allocation on quantum hardware: $+17.0 \pm 4.8$ pts at $N{=}20$ on \texttt{ibm\_aachen} ($3.5σ$, 5 seeds), with the advantage holding at $N{=}30$ at higher budget on \texttt{ibm\_berlin} ($+14.0 \pm 8.5$ pts, 5 seeds).

</details>


### [124] [ReMIA: a Powerful and Efficient Alternative to Membership Inference Attacks against Synthetic Data Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14686)
*Davide Scassola,Andrea Coser,Sebastiano Saccani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对表格数据合成中的隐私泄露问题，本文提出了一种名为 ReMIA 的高效隐私度量方法，它通过简单的相对比较机制，在大幅降低计算成本的同时实现了与顶尖攻击手段相当的检测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在共享表格数据时，现有的成员推理攻击（MIA）虽然强大但计算成本极高（依赖阴影建模和大量辅助数据），而现有的快速度量指标（如 DCR）又缺乏足够的灵敏度。因此，研究者迫切需要一种既灵敏又实用的隐私度量工具来评估合成数据的安全性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ReMIA（相对成员推理攻击）的隐私度量指标。该方法仅需两次 SDG 训练运行和与原始数据集等量的额外数据。其核心逻辑是生成两个基于不同源数据集的合成数据集，通过训练分类器来判断样本源自哪一个数据集，从而评估泄露风险。

Result: 实验结果表明，ReMIA 的检测灵敏度与现有最先进的 MIA 方法相当，但在计算资源和数据需求上表现出显著的实用优势。此外，研究发现 SDG 在平衡隐私保护与数据效用方面具有传统噪声技术无法比拟的优势。

Conclusion: ReMIA 是一种高效且实用的隐私评估指标，能够以极低的计算成本准确量化合成数据生成器（SDG）面临的成员推理攻击（MIA）风险，且证实了合成数据在隐私与效用平衡上优于传统的噪声添加式匿名化方法。

Abstract: Tabular data sharing under privacy constraints is increasingly important for research and collaboration. Synthetic data generators (SDGs) are a promising solution, but synthetic data remains vulnerable to attacks, such as membership inference attacks (MIAs), which aim to determine whether a specific record was part of the training data. State-of-the-art MIAs are powerful but impractical: they rely on shadow modeling, requiring hundreds of SDG training runs, and need auxiliary data several times larger than the original training set. Fast proxy metrics like distance to closest record (DCR) are efficient but have limited sensitivity to MIA risk. We introduce ReMIA (Relative Membership Inference Attack), a practical privacy metric that requires only two SDG training runs and additional data no larger than the original training set. Rather than predicting whether a record was in the training set, ReMIA generates two synthetic datasets from two source datasets and measures whether a classifier can identify which source a record came from. Experiments across multiple tabular datasets and SDGs show that ReMIA has a sensitivity comparable to state-of-the-art MIAs while being substantially more practical. We further observe that SDGs can achieve privacy-utility trade-offs that traditional noise-based anonymization methods do not match. Code is available at https://github.com/aindo-com/remia.

</details>


### [125] [Unsupervised learning of acquisition variability in structural connectomes via hybrid latent space modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13933)
*Gaurav Rudravaram,Lianrui Zuo,Karthik Ramadass,Elyssa McMaster,Jongyeon Yoon,Aravind R. Krishnan,Adam M. Saunders,Chenyu Gao,Nancy R. Newlin,Praitayini Kanakaraj,Lori L. Beason Held,Murat Bilgel,Laura A. Barquero,Micah DArchangel,Tin Q. Nguyen,Laurie B. Cutting,Derek Archer,Timothy J. Hohman,Daniel C. Moyer,Bennett A. Landman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用架构退火技术的混合深度学习框架，实现了对dMRI连接组数据中获取差异（扫描参数）与生物变异的自动、高效分离，显著提升了多中心成像数据的分析鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弥散磁共振成像（dMRI）的多中心数据在站点、扫描仪和成像协议上存在显著差异，导致结构连接组分析产生偏差。传统降维方法无法有效区分这些人为获取效应与真实的生物学变异，而现有的混合潜空间模型又往往需要复杂的手动调参，因此需要一种更智能、无需手动调节的自动化框架来分离这些混杂因素。

Method: 引入了一种无监督的混合潜空间深度学习框架，该框架通过在解码前对编码器输出进行“架构退火（architectural annealing）”，使模型能够在训练过程中自适应地平衡离散变量（用于捕获获取差异）和连续变量（用于捕获生物学变异），从而避免了传统模型中繁琐的手动容量调整。

Result: 在包含7,416个结构连接组的大规模数据集上测试表明，该框架在站点聚类任务上表现优异，其调整兰德系数（ARI）达到0.53（p<0.05），显著优于标准VAE、PCA+k-means以及基于损失函数退火的对比模型，有效实现了成像数据获取差异的自动识别与剥离。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于架构退火（Architectural Annealing）的无监督学习框架，能够有效将弥散磁共振成像（dMRI）数据中的获取差异（如扫描仪、协议）与生物学变异分离开来。研究证明，结合连续与离散变量的混合潜空间模型，通过架构层面的退火机制而非传统的损失函数退火，能更精准地捕获成像设备的系统性偏差，为大规模多中心神经影像分析提供了一种鲁棒的数据标准化与表示学习方法。

Abstract: Acquisition differences across sites, scanners, and protocols in dMRI introduce variability that complicates structural connectome analysis. This motivates deep learning models that can represent high-dimensional connectomes in a low-dimensional space while explicitly separating acquisition-related effects from biological variation. Conventional dimensionality reduction methods model all variance as continuous, so acquisition effects often get absorbed into a continuous latent space. Recent hybrid latent-space models combine discrete and continuous components to address this, but typically require manual capacity tuning to ensure the discrete component captures the intended variability. We introduce an unsupervised framework that removes this manual tuning by architecturally annealing encoder outputs before decoding, allowing the model to adaptively balance discrete and continuous latent variables during training. To evaluate it, we curated a dataset of N=7,416 structural connectomes derived from dMRI, spanning ages 2 to 102 and 13 studies with 25 unique acquisition-parameter combinations. Of these, 5,900 are cognitively unimpaired, 877 have mild cognitive impairment (MCI), and 639 have Alzheimer's disease (AD). We compare against a standard VAE, PCA with k-means clustering, and hybrid models that anneal only through the loss function. Our architectural annealing produces stronger site learning (ARI=0.53, p<0.05) than these baselines. Results show that a hybrid continuous-discrete latent space, with architectural rather than loss-based annealing, provides a useful unsupervised mechanism for capturing acquisition variability in dMRI: by jointly modeling smooth and categorical structure, the Joint-VAE recovers clusters aligned with scanner and protocol differences.

### [126] [The Rate-Distortion-Polysemanticity Tradeoff in SAEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14694)
*Tommaso Mencattini,Francesco Montagna,Francesco Locatello*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了稀疏自动编码器（SAE）在可解释性、重构精度与稀疏效率之间的“速率-失真-多义性权衡”，并论证了多义性主要由数据特征的共现模式所驱动，而非仅仅由模型架构决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稀疏自动编码器（SAE）在追求低重构误差（低失真）和高特征效率（低速率）时，往往无法学习到具有高度可解释性的“单义性”表示，限制了其在机制可解释性中的应用。研究者旨在刻画并解决这一在忠实度、效率与可解释性之间的权衡矛盾。

Method: 1. 引入“速率-失真-多义性权衡”（Rate-Distortion-Polysemanticity Tradeoff）理论框架；2. 在玩具模型（toy-modeling）假设下进行理论分析与实证测试，探究单义性约束对性能的影响；3. 基于生成模型分析特征共现概率如何决定多义性水平；4. 在未知数据生成过程的实际场景中，推导多义性度量的必要条件，并对大型语言模型（LLM）上的现有指标进行基准测试。

Result: 1. 证明了强制要求SAE保持单义性必然导致重构误差（失真）和编码复杂度（速率）的增加；2. 揭示了最优SAE的多义性程度主要由训练数据分布（特别是特征共现概率）决定；3. 评估了现有的多义性度量指标，并为在未知数据生成过程的情况下衡量多义性提供了必要条件。

Conclusion: 多义性（Polysemanticity）本质上是一个数据分布问题，而不仅仅是架构或优化问题。在寻求可解释性（单义性）时，必须在重构保真度（失真）、特征稀疏性（速率）与可解释性之间进行权衡。未来的研究应更多地关注数据特征的共现模式，以改进稀疏自动编码器的可解释性。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) that can accurately reconstruct their input (minimizing distortion) by making efficient use of few features (minimizing the rate) often fail to learn monosemantic representations (highly interpretable), limiting their usefulness for mechanistic interpretability. In this paper, we characterise this tension in learning faithful, efficient, and interpretable explanations, introducing the Rate-Distortion-Polysemanticity tradeoff in SAEs. Under toy-modeling assumptions, we theoretically and empirically show that restricting the SAE to be monosemantic necessarily comes with an increase in rate and distortion. Assuming a generative model behind the input observations, we further demonstrate that the degree of polysemanticity of optimal SAEs is determined by the training data distribution, especially by the probability of features to co-occur. Finally, we extend the analysis to real-world settings by deriving necessary conditions that a polysemanticity measure should satisfy when the data-generating process is unknown, and we benchmark existing proxy metrics on SAEs trained on Large Language Models. Taken together, our findings show that polysemanticity is a data problem that should be accounted for when addressing it at the architectural and optimization level.

### [127] [EvolveMem:Self-Evolving Memory Architecture via AutoResearch for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13941)
*Jiaqi Liu,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EvolveMem 是一种能够自我进化的 LLM 记忆架构，通过 LLM 驱动的闭环诊断与优化机制，自动调整检索配置以适应不同的任务需求，显著提升了智能体的记忆检索效能，并减少了人工调优需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 智能体记忆系统往往将检索基础设施视为固定的，即存储内容在更新，但检索逻辑、评分函数和生成策略在部署后无法改变。为了实现真正适应性强的长期记忆，需要存储知识与检索机制的双向协同进化。

Method: 提出了一种名为 EvolveMem 的自进化记忆架构。该系统将检索配置（如评分函数、融合策略等）暴露为结构化动作空间，并引入一个由 LLM 驱动的诊断模块。该模块通过分析失败日志来识别根因并进行配置调整，同时配合“防灾”元分析器（支持回归自动回滚和探索 stagnate 状态），实现了架构的自我迭代与演化。

Result: 在 LoCoMo 和 MemBench 基准测试中，EvolveMem 表现出色。在 LoCoMo 上，相比最强基线提升了 25.7%，相比最小基线提升了 78.0%；在 MemBench 上，较最强基线提升了 18.9%。此外，进化出的配置展现了良好的跨基准迁移能力，验证了其捕捉的是通用检索规律。

Conclusion: EvolveMem 证明了通过 LLM 驱动的闭环自我进化机制，大语言模型智能体能够自主优化其记忆检索策略。这种方法不仅取代了繁琐的人工调优，还揭示了通用的检索原则，能够跨任务进行有效的知识迁移。

Abstract: Long-term memory is essential for LLM agents that operate across multiple sessions, yet existing memory systems treat retrieval infrastructure as fixed: stored content evolves while scoring functions, fusion strategies, and answer-generation policies remain frozen at deployment. We argue that truly adaptive memory requires co-evolution at two levels: the stored knowledge and the retrieval mechanism that queries it. We present EvolveMem, a self-evolving memory architecture that exposes its full retrieval configuration as a structured action space optimized by an LLM-powered diagnosis module. In each evolution round, the module reads per-question failure logs, identifies root causes, and proposes targeted configuration adjustments; a guarded meta-analyzer applies them with automatic revert-on-regression and explore-on-stagnation safeguards. This closed-loop self-evolution realizes an AutoResearch process: the system autonomously conducts iterative research cycles on its own architecture, replacing manual configuration tuning. Starting from a minimal baseline, the process converges autonomously, discovering effective retrieval strategies including entirely new configuration dimensions not present in the original action space. On LoCoMo, EvolveMem outperforms the strongest baseline by 25.7% relative and achieves a 78.0% relative improvement over the minimal baseline. On MemBench, EvolveMem exceeds the strongest baseline by 18.9% relative. Evolved configurations transfer across benchmarks with positive rather than catastrophic transfer, indicating that the self-evolution process captures universal retrieval principles rather than benchmark-specific heuristics. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/SimpleMem.

### [128] [TAPIOCA: Why Task- Aware Pruning Improves OOD model Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14738)
*Krish Sharma,Omar Naim,Soumadeep Saha,Nicholas Asher*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了任务感知层剪枝之所以能提升模型OOD性能，是因为剪枝剔除了导致OOD输入表示几何失真的层，从而将数据重新校准至任务适配的几何空间中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究（如TALE）证明任务感知层剪枝能提升特定任务性能，但其背后的深层机制及其在何种条件下产生提升尚不明确，因此需要探索剪枝对分布内（ID）数据无效却对分布外（OOD）数据有效的根本原因。

Method: 研究人员通过受控的多项式回归任务和大规模语言模型，分析了剪枝前后的层级范数和成对距离分布。通过对比分布内（ID）与OOD输入的表示特征，提出了任务适应几何的概念，并利用因果证据（分布偏移和残差缩放干预）验证了剪枝机制。

Result: 实验表明，任务感知剪枝对ID数据无明显增益，但能稳定提升OOD准确率。OOD输入会导致模型表现出偏离ID数据的几何特征（范数和距离分布偏移），而剪枝通过移除放大该偏差的层，实现了对OOD表示的修正与对齐。

Conclusion: 任务感知剪枝通过去除导致分布外（OOD）输入表示失真的层，有效地将OOD数据的表示重新校准到模型已学习的任务适应几何空间中，从而提升模型泛化性能。

Abstract: Recent work has promoted task-aware layer pruning as a way to improve model performance on particular tasks, as shown by TALE. In this paper, we investigate when such improvements occur and why. We show first that, across controlled polynomial regression tasks and large language models, such pruning yields no benefit on in-distribution (ID) data but consistently improves out-of-distribution (OOD) accuracy. We further show empirically that OOD inputs induce layerwise norm and pairwise-distance profiles that deviate from the corresponding ID profiles. This leads to a geometric explanation of task-aware pruning: each task induces a task-adapted geometry, characterized empirically by the representation profiles observed on ID inputs. OOD inputs can introduce a distorted version of the task-adapted geometry. Task-aware pruning identifies layers that create or amplify this distortion; by removing them, it shifts OOD representational norms and pairwise distances toward those observed on the adapted distribution. This realigns OOD inputs with the model's task-adapted geometry and improves performance. We provide causal evidence through controlled distribution shifts and residual-scaling interventions, and demonstrate consistent behavior across model scales.

### [129] [Collider-Bench: Benchmarking AI Agents with Particle Physics Analysis Reproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13950)
*Darius A. Faroughy,Sofia Palacios Schweitzer,Ian Pang,Siddharth Mishra-Sharma,David Shih*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究推出了Collider-Bench，这是一个旨在测试语言模型智能体复现大型强子对撞机（LHC）科学分析能力的基准，结果显示当前智能体在处理复杂的领域任务时仍难以达到人类专家水平。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体基准测试难以捕捉真实科学工作的复杂性和细微差别。科学分析通常难以复现，因为公开工具链往往不完整，且论文常遗漏关键实现细节，需要智能体具备物理推理和试错能力来填补空白。

Method: 提出了Collider-Bench基准测试，要求智能体利用公开论文和开源科学软件复现大型强子对撞机（LHC）的实验分析。智能体需构建可执行的模拟与选择流水线并预测碰撞事件产量，评估方式包括标准的直方图指标和基于LLM的评估器来检测幻觉和编造等定性失败模式，同时记录计算成本。

Result: 实验表明，目前参与测评的通用编程智能体在处理此类高难度科学任务时表现不佳，尚未有任何智能体能够可靠地超越由物理学家参与（human-in-the-loop）的解决方案。

Conclusion: 当前的通用大语言模型智能体在执行复杂的科学分析任务时，仍无法稳定超越人类物理学家的水平。该研究强调了在处理真实世界科学任务时，模型在领域知识应用、物理推理以及应对信息缺失方面的局限性。

Abstract: Autonomous language-model agents are increasingly evaluated on long-horizon tool-use tasks, but existing benchmarks rarely capture the complexity and nuance of real scientific work. To address this gap, we introduce Collider-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating whether LLM agents can reproduce experimental analyses from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) using only public papers and open scientific software. Such analyses are often difficult to reproduce because the public toolchain only approximates the software used internally by the experimental collaborations, while the published papers inevitably omit implementation details needed for a faithful reconstruction. Agents must therefore rely on physical reasoning, domain knowledge, and trial-and-error to fill these gaps. Each task requires the agent to turn a published analysis into an executable simulation-and-selection pipeline and submit predicted collision event yields in specified signal regions. These predictions are evaluated with standard histogram metrics that provide continuous fidelity scores without a hand-written rubric. We also report the computational cost incurred by each agent per task. Finally, we evaluate the codebase and full session trace using an LLM judge to catch qualitative failure modes such as fabrications, hallucinations and duplications. We release an initial set of tasks drawn from LHC searches, together with a containerized sandbox and event simulation tools. We evaluate across a capability ladder of general purpose coding agents. Our results show that on average no agent reliably beats the physicist-in-the-loop solution.
